**Selected Words of Reverend Sun Myung Moon**  
63  
**Compilation Committee of Reverend Sun Myung Moon's Words**  

**Foreword**  
**President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo**

1)  
**Our Purpose**  
<Prayer> Loving Father! Today is October 1, 1972, a morning that marks the end of three-quarters of the year and the beginning of the last three months. May you bless us on this first day of the month. This day is also the Sabbath, a time when we must devote our hearts and bodies with sincerity. From a principled perspective, it is also the first day that surpasses the number nine and enters into ten.  
We know that this year is a historically significant year in which we must determine the fate of history. As we enter October, may you look upon us with compassion and allow us to be a group of children who possess the justification necessary to stand before your heart and will. May we reaffirm this morning our determination to be a group that can add to your hopes and expectations in every aspect you desire.  
Father! The reason we have pioneered this path is that there is still a way for you to go. Therefore, we have traced the path of pioneering to arrive at this point. Father! When we think that yesterday was a struggle, today is a struggle, and tomorrow will also be a struggle, we must once again consider how much you, who bear the destiny of history, must suffer, be lonely, and endure pain. The more difficult our path becomes, the more we must look up to heaven, comfort ourselves, and lead ourselves again on the path of restoration that remains until this day, October 1, 1972, at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
*This message was also published in the August 1973 issue of <Unification World>.*  
8 **Our Purpose**  
We earnestly hope that you will illuminate all our paths and grant us strength and ability so that we can become your children who can overcome the final summit.  
As time goes on, we are becoming increasingly aware of the magnitude of the mission we must undertake. The global situation is surrounding us, drawing closer and closer. When we contemplate the path this nation must take in the future, we realize that it is a lonely nation that cannot overcome all these circumstances with human strength alone. While the North and South are at odds, we recognize that the historical fate surrounding this land, centered on South Korea, is a dead end that cannot be resolved by human effort alone. We also see that the destiny of Christianity, spread across the world, is heading down a similar path.  
We feel that rather than trying to solve problems by asserting ourselves, we must embrace heaven, hoping for the authority, mercy, and compassion of heaven to manifest, and seek heaven's mercy through historical repentance.  
Father! Please encourage the young children gathered here once again at this time. You, who regard each life as precious! They are yearning for your nation of liberation and victory where they can reside.  
They are persevering, hoping for the time when they can participate in your victory, and unless you lead them to that place, they will not be able to partake in your wondrous grace due to their own human shortcomings. We realize that it is only natural that without your guidance and support, we cannot participate in such a place.  
Now we must present ourselves entirely before you, so that you can once again have compassion, love, and a heart of mercy to protect us. We must reaffirm that this is the path we must take.  
9  
Father! At this time, hold us and guide us on our path.  
Now we have entered October. This season is the autumn season when all things look forward to harvest. Wouldn't it be wonderful if this season could remove the historical sorrow? After autumn, winter will come, and even if we face harsh and merciless conditions, we know too well that unless we become seeds with our own life force, we cannot seek the connection of new sprouts that will be sown in the spring garden.  
We feel that each of our lives must become a solid fruit in the face of this era, which is the harvest time of human history. As autumn approaches, we must possess the essence of life that can cling to it and suppress all environmental conditions.  
It is not by anyone else's strength that we will be protected, but we must maintain our life force and break through difficult environments with our own strength and nutrition. This trial period, like winter, has come to this nation and this world, or to many religious circles. At this time, how many entities with true historical fruits of life are there that heaven is seeking? We understand that this is your concern, your desire, and the object of your hope during the harvest time.  
We hope that this time will become a moment for us to feel once again that we must be those very entities today. We earnestly wish for this realization.  
Look upon your children gathered here. How many sons and daughters are there in your heart who cannot be forgotten, and how many are there who can participate in pioneering the path you desire? How many warriors can you trust and present in your battlefields? If there are any, may they pledge their essential thoughts and their resolved hearts of loyalty and filial piety, so that they may become unforgettable beings in your heart. If they become the sons and daughters you expect and desire, they will inevitably be able to anticipate new hopes, new expectations, and victories.  
10 **Our Purpose**  
When there are such children here, please encourage them. We earnestly ask that you raise many who will bear the responsibility for the nation and the world, inheriting the will of heaven, which has been responsible for everything until now.  
Have compassion on the multitude that has come this morning. May this be a time when we humbly dedicate our hearts and bodies before you. As we reflect on what position we are in now, let us consider how much difference there is between your desired standard and how much alignment we have with it. May this morning be a time for us to return to you and to establish ourselves once again for you.  
We earnestly ask that you protect our path as we must run the busy course of restoration centered on the task of safeguarding the unification front. Please remember the groups of unification scattered around the world, and may you love the mobile units fighting at the forefront in various countries. In Korea, your young daughters are fighting on the front lines, so please have compassion on their paths, responsibilities, and missions. Bless every place where we gather today in your name, and may your grace and mercy overflow there. We earnestly ask that you take charge of everything.  
Now, in this last period of this year, with only three months left in October, November, and December, we earnestly hope that everything we plan in accordance with your will will progress rapidly. Mobilize the countless spirits in the spirit world so that they can work alongside the good descendants on this earth to establish a new nation and a new world. Father, grant them the privilege to act on behalf of the earth directly, so that everything can culminate in the world you desire. Please bless and guide us so that goodness can delineate a new dividing line and confirm the results of your eternal victory.  
11  
We earnestly ask that the grace of ten thousand blessings be with the groups of unification and all people. We pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.  
**Words**: We are a group that proudly identifies as members of the Unification Church. We understand that the Unification Church is a new religious organization.  
**The Purpose of Religion**  
There are countless religions in this world. We know that these religions seek the highest purpose and strive to attain it. This is achieved through true people. Many religions have emerged throughout history as true people come together to pursue the true purpose.  
Then, the concept of truth or the purpose of religion should not be diverse. Regardless of the historical flow, even if a religion exists within a certain generational sphere, when viewed from the perspective of a higher purpose that connects the past and the future, it is certain that even if there are many religions, they must converge through one path to reach one world of purpose.  
However, even when looking at Christianity, there are many denominations. Buddhism also has many sects. Even when we consider the world religions we know, there are many sects. So what is the purpose of the emergence of so many sects? It undoubtedly originates from an internal demand to affirm a better purpose and to realize that better purpose within their own sectarian boundaries.  
Therefore, even if disputes arise between sects, they should not be a regression of the current advancing position but rather a dispute aimed at elevating the dimension. However, when this does not happen, the purposes of the disputing sects stand in opposition to each other.  
12 **Our Purpose**  
No matter how large a religion may be, it is undeniable that it aims toward one supreme purpose. We know that the purpose of religion, or the path taken centered on religion, originates from the absolute God. The only God they worship is the one who can ultimately emerge as the victorious God in this universe, and through the doctrines or scriptures presented through their sect, they are living a faith that will inevitably lead to one world of victory. However, there cannot be two gods. There can only be one God. What that God desires is one purpose and one result.  
**Purpose Orientation Must Be in One Direction**  
From this perspective, the path that many religions must take is to reach the place of purpose as quickly as possible. That is the issue. Even when we look at athletes on a racetrack, the process of running from the start to reaching the goal is a competition and a struggle. However, if they look sideways while running, those two individuals cannot be seen as having the correct purpose and mission as runners in that race. In a struggle, it is acceptable to compete with a shared purpose from the start, but if one engages in disputes by focusing on oneself and looking sideways at others, they will inevitably taste the sorrow of defeat.  
Only in fighting should one fight for their purpose. Isn't it busy to fight toward the purpose? A person who looks sideways and worries about others while fighting will inevitably face the path of defeat.  
Similarly, when we look at the many religions spread across the world, we see that they have been competing with each other. In the past, Christianity was often referred to as the dominant religion, while Buddhism and others were labeled as foreign religions. They have fought from an antagonistic position against other religions. If one religion completely reaches its intended purpose and judges another religion as wrong, it may gain authority that can be recognized, but fighting from a position that has not reached its goal does not help the path of religions that are striving toward their goals.  
While such struggles have continued, we are also aware that many sects within numerous religions have split and fought. The more these struggles increase, the less they lead to results that promote advancement and affirm purpose; rather, they only serve to confuse the path and strengthen the negative aspects regarding direction and purpose.  
This is not only true for religions but also for nations. When all citizens of a nation thoroughly look toward one purpose and strive together with a unified mindset, regardless of their positions, including leaders and citizens, that nation will develop. There will be progress. However, no matter how great the purpose may be, when horizontal struggles and antagonistic reactions occur, stagnation is inevitable. This does not end with a single struggle; even if one wins a fight, another challenger will appear to influence them, and even if they defeat that challenger, another will emerge to exert influence, ultimately leading to their weakening.  
Therefore, for those who look toward a purpose, horizontal struggles or conflicts signify depletion and result in a decrease in the power to advance. In other words, rather than presenting the necessary requirements toward the purpose, they reach a result that deprives those requirements, which is beyond dispute.  
This applies not only to a single sect but also to a nation. Furthermore, when we look at the global situation, the same is true. The democratic world and the communist world are currently in conflict. The democratic world aspires to an ideal world.
is a matter of perspective. The communist world is also striving towards a desired ideal world centered around communism, fighting from a conflicting standpoint. 

The issue is whether they can reach that goal and establish the desired ideal world or the authority that achieves that goal. When fighting laterally or in all directions, the opposing subjects must ultimately submit before the achievement of the goal itself. A world that fights without reaching the intended result does not provide hope, desire, or a clear future for all humanity and the entire world; rather, it confuses and disrupts the path forward, as we observe in today's reality.

This is similarly true for individuals. Once a person has determined a specific goal, they should invest all their energy and direct all their efforts toward that goal, shortening the distance to it the more they engage. However, if they engage in various lateral struggles while having a grand goal, the original goal becomes increasingly unclear, and the path to achieving that goal becomes more distant.

To achieve the goal, one must invest everything. From this perspective, since God knows very well the purpose humans should pursue, He must demand that we head straight toward that goal. Even if humans find themselves in such a position, if they earnestly pursue that path and intensify their gradual struggle, they can follow that goal. However, if they engage in lateral developments, the momentum toward the goal will gradually fade. God, who knows this all too well, cannot help but teach humans to advance along a single path.

Therefore, as long as God exists, there is a responsibility to clearly indicate that path to humanity. When we examine the Bible, we see that God has instructed us to devote all our sincerity to fulfill His will through His love, to dedicate and invest everything without holding anything back, urging us to run toward that goal.

Thus, the Bible states, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your might." There is nothing beyond this. Of course, if there are other matters, they come after achieving this, and God would not want to resolve them in a position where He is involved in His purpose. The more thorough one is in their purpose, the more thorough they must be in their direction. If a purpose can only be accomplished once, there is no room for practice. If there is no practice, how serious and thorough must it be?

What we often do tends to lead to failure. From this understanding, if there is a most precious purpose that must be accomplished only once, and if there is a God who presents that purpose, how serious must God be in presenting that purpose? The greater the purpose, the more resolve, strength, and content must be instilled in the person to overcome and fulfill that purpose.

Since there can be no failure on the path to that purpose, and since it is a purpose that must be accomplished only once, if there are beloved children or loved ones responsible for that purpose, how serious must the urging be? It is indeed true that they must not be distracted, and it is also true that they must be encouraged to keep going without rest, cutting off all desires that a human might wish for and urging them to focus solely on that purpose.

From this perspective, the ultimate purpose we humans must pursue is indeed the most serious purpose. Your life is not a path that can be corrected if you stray. If a day has passed, that day has forever parted from you. If a year has passed, that year has forever parted from you. When considering whether I am advancing or retreating over the course of a year regarding a purpose that can only be achieved through a single action, the question of how much that advancement truly was will measure the value of that year. Or, when considering how much one has advanced toward that purpose through youth or adulthood, everyone desires to achieve this in a short time. This desire is universal, regardless of one's abilities or age.

Values are determined around the purpose. Therefore, to achieve that purpose in a short time, the proportional investment of strength and time is inevitable. Thus, in achieving any purpose, especially during youth, the question is how much one has advanced with all their strength during that period—not retreating, but advancing. The differences in position regarding the purpose will determine the recognition of value.

As you know, in a marathon, many people run, but the one who leads from the start is recognized for their value based on the goal of being first. Therefore, even when listening to a broadcast, we hear who is leading from the starting line. The question becomes how much effort they have made to be in the lead and who is closest to the goal.

If a year has passed, the question of how meaningful that year was is not simply because it was 1972. If there is a purpose that our Unification Church desires in 1972, despite many years having passed in history, the question is how much we have shortened the distance to that purpose compared to other years. This is undeniable.

Thus, in your daily life, saying "I felt good today" or "I was lucky today" is the same. While one may not be entirely aware, it is true that we are secretly pursuing happiness in life. If there is a heavenly fortune, it undoubtedly drives all humanity toward that place. While some may be standing aside or going backward, the fact remains that everyone is heading in that direction.

However, even if everyone stands in line, the ultimate goal converges to a single point. No matter how large the goal is, when viewed from the internal and external aspects of that goal, there is only one path to the relative existence that the goal desires. If a person can achieve that goal, there are not two paths they can take. There is only one way to reach it. 

Of course, there may be many paths surrounding a central line, but there is only one way for the goal and the target it seeks to meet. This single path, the straight line, determines how much it can be shortened and how close it can get to the goal. The farther away it is, the more distant the position that can achieve that goal becomes.

When viewed from the perspective of our Unification Church, there is only one path toward the goal. It is indeed a single path, not two. There cannot be two paths. If there is a leader running at the forefront, they wish to head straight toward the goal. Regardless of spring, summer, autumn, or winter, they must run straight. Each of the 365 days that make up spring, summer, autumn, and winter must also run straight.

Daily life must also be directed toward that straight line, whether in the morning, at lunch, or in the evening. Even if I am doing something else elsewhere, the direction of that work must also be toward the straight path. When people work in such a position and engage in relative tasks that align with the goal every day, it becomes a joyful experience. When that alignment is lost, joy cannot exist. No matter how happy today may be, if it conflicts with the ultimate goal, we cannot help but find ourselves in the sorrowful position of a loser. This is undeniable.

Thus, all statements about being good or bad, happy or unlucky, are ultimately determined based on the central purpose of life, not based on personal feelings or daily circumstances. It is undoubtedly based on a single purpose, following the internal connections that one aims for, determining what is good or bad. If one claims something is good without that purpose, no matter how good it seems, it becomes equivalent to something bad. From this perspective, we must engage in our faith life.

We are heading toward a single purpose. Even if South Korea is currently thriving and can boast about it, the path South Korea takes must not be solely for the people of South Korea. If that happens, there may be hopes for South Korea, but it cannot reach the hopes of the entire world. Therefore, what can allow South Korea to rejoice forever? While it would be nice if there are things that the nation and its people can rejoice in from the current perspective, if that joy does not align with the path of the nation's destiny toward the world, then that joy may ultimately be less than the sorrow of worrying about today's problems for tomorrow's world.

From this perspective, the Unification Church itself is no different today. We must first determine whether the path we are on is the right one. Upon entering the Unification Church, one must decide whether this path is certain or incorrect. Is it a path that humanity can originally take? Is it a path that everyone, regardless of age or gender, can take? Is it a path that only those within the limits of the Unification Church should follow, or is it a path that all of humanity must take beyond South Korea? Is it a path that only those representing humanity can take, or is there another path if there is a heavenly principle beyond human principles?

When human principles and heavenly principles diverge, we should follow the heavenly principle. However, if we step forward solely for human principles while setting aside heavenly principles, then at that point, we must turn back toward the heavenly path. The issue lies here. The closer we get to the goal, the more the value of that purpose increases. Therefore, as the goal approaches, there can only be a straight path without any wavering. Isn't that right, everyone? The person running toward the finish line focuses all their thoughts on that finish line. All actions converge around that finish line. As the time for the purpose approaches, everything must be invested. Even if one is in pain, the plea of "I'm in pain, please understand" does not apply. In that moment, whether it is a minute or a second, which is extremely short in the span of a lifetime, it is a breathtaking finish line that can erase all infinite value.

As you see in sports, in the end, it is not just a matter of a single step. A tenth of a step, a hundredth of a step—if there is even a slight distance, first and second place become worlds apart. If first place is the sky, then second place must be the ground. If first place is a high mountain, then second place must stand in a relative position to that. The difference in those moments becomes significant at the finish line. If someone can commit to that serious moment throughout their life, they will undoubtedly walk the right path.

Therefore, if we invest our sincerity, we must do so with the same heart as in the final moments looking toward the finish line, from the very start. If someone invests themselves in that tense position throughout their life, even if they do not achieve first place, they can still receive an encouragement award.

We humans have a path in life. In pursuing the path of destiny that we can take as humans, we are all heading toward a common purpose. There are many sects, but their purpose is singular: to achieve that one purpose. Whether it is world peace or a unified world, we are all running toward the culmination of an ideal world, toward that goal. Thus, no matter how many organizations there are, they must not run separately. In other words, it is like fingers; the ten fingers must not fight. If they fight, nothing will be accomplished.

The opposition to the Unification Church is a developmental phenomenon. The Unification Church has emerged as a new religious group in this world. It has gone through decades of history, during which there have been many difficulties. There have been personal struggles, family struggles, and trials faced in all dealings, which were not merely challenges arising from habitual environments throughout one's life. Individuals have faced trials solely because they believe in the Unification Church. Families have faced trials. The entire church has been undergoing trials. While the Unification Church has faced trials, it has also caused trials for others. 

If the Unification Church did not exist, it might have been better, but by its emergence, it has become a subject of concern for established churches. Whether they like it or not, they have entered a stage where they must study it. Thus, while we have faced persecution personally, within families, socially, and within the church, that does not end with just our own experiences. The path we take inevitably influences the surrounding conditions. By walking this path, your families are facing trials from opposing positions. 

Is that a bad thing or a good thing? If there is an athlete, until they are recognized as an athlete, their efforts alone are not enough. Those connected to the sport must support them from behind. Even in that support, it is a matter of perspective.
is. Depending on how much of a cooperative environment one has, the more such a foundation one has, the quicker they will achieve success. Isn't that right? What that means is that when an athlete is growing, it is not enough for just that athlete to put in effort. For an athlete to emerge, all the conditions related to them, such as their parents, siblings, and friends, must be able to cooperate and put in the same effort. The more such an environment one has, the quicker they can achieve success. Until an athlete becomes well-known as an athlete, both they themselves and their surrounding environment must endure suffering. This is an inevitable developmental phenomenon.

Today, the Unification Church has faced opposition, whether good or bad. It is not only the Unification Church that faces opposition and suffering. The family members of those who belong to the Unification Church also face opposition and suffering. They oppose not because they are aligned with the same purpose but because they are in a conflicting position, and they are suffering as a result.

Then, there is the question of who stands in a more valuable position between those who oppose and those who are opposed. The more extreme the opposition, the more valuable the person who overcomes that opposition becomes. If the path they are taking is the true path, does their value decrease the more opposition they face? No, it is the opposite. The more opposition there is from the environment, the more the person who is being opposed stands in a better position. The more true that position is, the more severe the opposing environment is, the more valuable that person becomes as they walk that path.

Our Purpose
One must sacrifice oneself to advance towards the common good of humanity.

If one is pursuing their own purpose, they will not face opposition. The very fact of facing opposition from parents, siblings, and the living environment up until now indicates that it is not for their own purpose. They are facing opposition not from the position they have maintained until now but because they have broken free from the habitual environment they have lived in. Ultimately, they are being opposed as a different self than before, not as the same self as before. This stands at the extremes.

If yesterday was like that, then facing opposition is like this. Until yesterday, one absolutely obeyed their parents, but today they are in a position to make their parents obey them. Who is at the center of this? If one stands in a position to make their parents, siblings, or anyone else submit, that is not acceptable. That is not permissible. Rather, one must represent a higher nation and the world and seek to make them submit from that position.

Because it is a position where such a purpose is established, one faces opposition to involve that purpose's value. Ultimately, who is it for? It is not for oneself but for the other, which leads to a guaranteed good.

What is good? It is not about trying to make the world submit for oneself. It is about having the highest purpose at the center and trying to make others submit to that purpose. The path that pursues good is achieved through such results. Therefore, trying to make others submit to the purpose centered on good is always good.

For this reason, private and public matters have different directions. Private matters seek to draw others in and make them submit to oneself, while public matters seek to sacrifice oneself to be made to submit. That is opposition. Then why is the public good? By doing so, I can advance. If I try to draw others in and advance while they are attached to me, I become like a person carrying a burden. I should shed the burden and be directed towards the purpose, yet I become someone who is weighed down by the burden without regard for the purpose. Greed ultimately leads to self-destruction.

That is why religious teachings emphasize meekness, humility, and sacrifice. Stand on the public path, for only on the public path can the liberation rights of all individuals and another purpose that can liberate them be connected. If one centers everything around oneself, the common purpose that humanity desires disappears. The position that emerges after sacrificing oneself creates a path to approach the common purpose that humanity desires. Therefore, private matters lead to evil, while public matters lead to the good that the world hopes for.

The achievement of the purpose of good is through sacrifice and love.

What kind of God is the God of good? He is a God of sacrifice and love. Love cannot exist apart from the essence of sacrifice. Sacrificing for the one you love does not mean that sacrifice is not considered a sacrifice. The more one sacrifices, the more fulfillment they feel. Love has such a distinct nature. When considering how great love is, the place that expresses it must be determined by how great the amount of sacrifice is. The greater the sacrifice, the greater the love expressed; the less the sacrifice, the lesser the love expressed.

Parents from poor families, who cannot feed or clothe their children like others, and cannot do the things they want for their children, suffer more deeply than wealthy parents who do well by their children. Therefore, the heart that goes through each moment of dealing with their children is incomparable to the love of wealthy parents for their children.

In the eyes of those parents, tears accompany their gaze. Emotions always burst forth. The person standing in that position, no matter how miserable they may be, cannot say, "You must sacrifice for me." Instead, they say, "I must do more for you." Rather, such a position does not prompt despair; the more they are in that position, the more they say, "Oh! Just endure a little longer! There will come a time when you can do things like others. If that time does not come, I will pray to God for strength!"

Therefore, not all children from difficult families are unhappy. Historical figures have often grown up under the love of harsh parents rather than wealthy ones. The more patriotic the parents who love their country, the more their children, nurtured by that love, can become patriots who will build the future of their nation. The birth of patriots occurs there.

Private matters only bring laughter in the present. Who do they laugh with? It is not with others but with oneself. Everyone should understand that happiness is not achieved alone. The very concept of happiness is relational. The word "good" is not achieved alone. The degree of joy is determined by how much one mobilizes relative relationships.

When something good happens, everyone wants to boast about it globally, right? But when something bad happens, they want to hide it from the world. Do you know why? They hope it will disappear. They do not want to reveal it to anyone. Seeking a value that they do not want to reveal is an act for oneself. The flow of results that arises through greed cannot occupy such a position. No matter how much one can boast about the results they have achieved, they cannot boast. However, if they have done such things for others and for the whole, even if they are in a lowly, despicable, or unspeakable position, they become more dignified the higher they go. In this regard, the paths of good and evil are intertwined.

Therefore, achieving the purpose and fulfilling the will cannot be done by those who seek today's happiness and satisfaction centered around themselves. The path that pursues a greater purpose of good... Those who are satisfied with the present and seek comfort for themselves become the losers.

Religion presents the path to God quickly.

How much effort do marathon runners exert while running? They struggle to breathe, feel overwhelmed, and teeter on the edge of collapse while overcoming those challenges. "Oh, I’m struggling; why should I run? Ah! What’s the point of running in the heat of summer? I should rest comfortably." Those who think like this, no matter how much they trumpet their success and say, "Follow me, and you will succeed; follow me, and you will achieve your purpose," do not believe it. Only those who run with all their might, even in the hottest weather, will inherit that purpose. Isn’t that so?

Those who place their purpose before them and seek comfort for themselves are exceedingly foolish. They are destined to fail. It is natural for them to drink from the cup of defeat. If such a person stands in a position representing the nation, it becomes a disgrace to the country. Even if they come in last, if they run with all their strength and collapse at the finish line, they may not be first, but they become a hero in that event. That is possible.

It is not about being first. It is about how much effort one has put in, how much sincerity and life they have invested in that path. The measurement of distance determines the value, and the measurement of that person's sincerity influences the value. Through such events, we can clearly see that our path of faith is similar.

Therefore, we must run quickly. We must run quickly, day and night. If someone with religious talent runs quickly and comes in first, that would be great, but even if they do not come in first, if they have put in many times the effort of the first-place runner, they can create a legacy in history. It is more desirable that someone who has not been talented but has put in sincere effort becomes first. 

When comparing someone with talent to someone without talent, the one without talent may come in first. Then, who can move history? The one who follows sincerity may not come in first, but if the one with talent comes in with a sense of shame, then the one who followed sincerity must teach the path of sincerity.

The path of religion presents such a content-driven journey. Even if one cannot run fast, God needs those who, even if they come in last, run with all their strength and sincerity, sacrificing their lives for the whole. God does not only look at the outline. God seeks the world of the original form. It is not just about going; one must go and return. To return, one must prepare another door. If one has gone this way, they must return from the other side. Therefore, one cannot rely solely on one direction. There must be sincerity.

That is why the Bible says, "Pray without ceasing," and "Run without ceasing." Such contradictory content exists. If one prays without ceasing, how can they run? You must understand that the reason for presenting such conflicting content is that there are two sides to it. No matter how much talent one has and comes in first, they must return. To return, they must run back. Therefore, one must become a qualified person who can support and uphold that achievement. If there is a way to liberate the world through being beggars and living as the lowest of the low, then we must also comply and go. We have brought this upon ourselves because we hope there is no such path, and we have played the role of beggars and servants. We are the Unification Church group that has pioneered the path of suffering.  
Father, now you must protect South Korea. Father, who knows that it is a pitiful nation in Asia, you must not become a Father who turns away from this land, carrying the sorrow of having come to this land during the historical era.  
Even if it is just one life, there must be someone who serves Heaven. How much have you longed for there to be a master who can welcome you by preparing a warm room on a cold winter night? When I think that a thousand years of history begins in that room, families of the Unification Church must serve Heaven, discuss in secret, and receive missions in secret. We must become a group that pledges loyalty and filial duty before the Father as a group with grievances, and that group must become the group of unification.  
We have fought for the nation. Although the Unification Church is in a humble position, we have fought for the nation. Father, I know well that there can be no situation where the nation we have fought for disappears. Even if we enter a place where we could perish, if there is even one person who clings to that nation until the end, we believe that we can overcome suffering, and in the future, a new path of revival will be filled before this nation, so I have come this far. Father, please take care of South Korea!  
Please protect this Korea, which stands like a young orphan in the historical flow of North and South being at odds with each other. The groups of unification that are being mocked among the Koreans, those who have been crying out for the nation must not become weary. Standing in a dignified position, they must be remembered in the Father’s heart along with sorrow and remain as warriors of remembrance who pledge for the future. If such people can become the group of unification, we believe that the wishes we desire can surely be fulfilled on this earth, so we must become a group that can be remembered before your heart.  
Father, now please protect the latter half of 1972. I hope that through these three months, there will be a way to pledge Heaven’s victory. I hope that a historical transition will take place during the three-year period until 1974. I sincerely hope that each of us will be allowed to invest all our sincerity for this one purpose. When we think that there is no other foundation for our hopes than to endure and overcome this suffocating period and this choking environment, each individual of the nation must unite here, and the entire nation must unite to... Our Standard Point  
<Prayer> Today is October 8th, this month is the month of harvest, and today is the second Sabbath of this month.  
Father, in the course of our faith life over the passing days, we feel that the days are moving toward the latter half of 1972 while raising the will you desire and pledging the life path we must take.  
In the morning, we greet the morning sunlight without fail and spend each day while seeking a fresh life path and a new value. Father, you must know very well our appearances as we spend each day.  
The children gathered here have various hearts and shapes of mind. Father, looking at this, we must be able to respond with the original posture that you can find, that you can come upon, and that you can rejoice in, and we must become sons and daughters who can harmonize, be at peace, and be in your presence. Thus, we must become children who can feel that you are watching over our appearances with a refined inner heart.  
We must know what value standard your words, which you command when you open your mouth, establish for each of us. We must understand what direction you are pointing to. Father, we must establish our position and be able to march directly toward the destination you designate, and we must not fail to embody the true sons and daughters you desire, so we have come to this place with that hope.  
Father, this place is the headquarters of the Unification Church. Therefore, we must truly understand that this is a place that many children long for with their hearts and that many people from various nations admire.  
This place is not only entrusted with a precious mission by Heaven but is also a place where we hope to pledge a new historical origin. When we think of this, we understand that this is a place given by Heaven, a place given by humans, and a place where we must bear the responsibility to march directly toward your will without deviation while serving Heaven and living as humans. Therefore, Father, we must have a clear sense of purpose.  
We must be those who clearly understand that without establishing an undeniable direction in our daily lives regarding that purpose, we cannot walk the true path of life.  
We must not spend countless days just passing them as they are. We must become a holy group that can yearn for and stand in a position that can change and transform to align with your heart. We have already known that we want to meet and find such a group through your will.  
We, the Unification group, know very well that many ancestors in history could not overcome the path of suffering they sought in the dark and left behind a lament of sorrow as they flowed with history. Now we pledge that we must not tread the same path as our ancestors. They did not go that way because they wanted to. They struggled with all their might, but they reached such a result and flowed with a sad history.  
We must become the object of consolation with Heaven at the place where we should establish the true path of faith, but because we could not dedicate that place before Heaven, we left behind a historical mark of sorrow.  
Moreover, that mark has remained as a mark of all heavenly grievances and has become the origin of inheriting the conditions of sorrow. We must become children who can once again engrave this painful truth in our hearts.  
When we call you Father, that Father must not be an abstract father. We must look directly at you and follow the direction you are going. We should not be pleased if that path is smooth; even if it is a path filled with suffering, we must feel that it is the path of the parents, so we must follow that path as a duty of the children.  
We must overcome the path of suffering of the individual and pioneer the path of suffering of the family, and we must overcome the path of suffering of the family and pioneer the path of the tribe, and we must think of the path of restoration that advances toward the nation, the state, and the world.  
Father, the children gathered here today must clarify what position each of them is in. Have we not yet broken the chains that bind us? Are we groaning in the trap we are caught in? If anyone wishes to be saved, they must look up to you and absolutely obey the voice that comes down from above. Otherwise, we will not be able to attain the appearance of liberation from our current environment. If we are trapped, we must look up and seek the one path...
must not be left behind. If one is bound by shackles, one cannot break free without finding something new that can sever those bonds, without possessing some new equipment to do so. When considering the fact that if one does not possess what can sever those bonds, one cannot have an environment of liberation, one must understand the position of one's own credibility. If I have been liberated, I should be able to hope for the liberation of my family, tribe, and nation, yet we are all too aware that we are fragile and weak beings who cannot stand in such a position. We must advance, yet we hesitate to move forward; we must fight for tomorrow's hope, yet we are aware that we tend to evade the struggle.

80 Our Standard Point
When we look to pursue something better than our current position, even if we have something better at that position, if that position is not what heaven desires and not where we should be, we must recognize that no matter how good a position we may have been granted, it will simply slip away and cannot establish a relationship with us. If we settle into a position that we deem good, believing it to be where we want to be, that position will become a place of bondage from which we can never attain eternal liberation. As we elevate our dimensions, we must recognize that we are on a sorrowful path of return that must traverse from the individual to the family, to the tribe, to the nation, and to the world. We must realize that without struggling to embrace our individual life paths, we are the descendants of corruption. Acknowledging this painful truth, we must fight with a heart of lamentation.

We must overcome today’s self and strive to affirm tomorrow’s self, sacrificing and overcoming today’s self for that day. We must learn to pull our hesitant bodies forward, placing a more progressive self before us rather than simply following our current selves. I earnestly hope and desire that you allow us to feel this truth. Father, please watch over us who have come to this place. What position are we in now? Are we standing for our nation? Are we standing for the world? Father, are we standing in place of the whole? Please allow us to feel once more whether we are worthy of the calling that comes to us, saying, "Hey, you, take on this responsibility."

Father, we humbly bow down, hoping for your mercy and the grace of your compassion to be poured out upon us. We are pitiful beings who cannot do anything on our own, and we are in a position of lamentation for our bound selves. You know this well, and you have mobilized countless saints in the spiritual world for our sake. Even though we may face conditions of suffering that could tire us from repeated mobilization, you have continued to mobilize numerous spirits in the spiritual realm for us. We earnestly ask that you send spiritual ancestors whom you can love to this earth to assist us in paving the way according to your command.

I know that it is impossible for me to be liberated on my own. I must open up spiritually, receive direct commands from heaven, and establish a self that can respond to those commands and absolutely comply with the subject. Without doing so, I cannot attain the right of liberation. Therefore, Father, I earnestly hope and desire that you guide us directly, protect us, nurture us, and if we are stagnant in our shortcomings, allow us to advance toward you even if it means striking us with a whip. 

If we are in a position of mission yet seek comfort and ease, please take everything away and allow us to cross this path, even if it means giving us double the pain. We know that without this, we cannot properly walk the path we must take. We entrust everything to you, and we earnestly hope and desire that you lead us until we become victorious figures who can respond to your wishes.

Father, please remember all your children scattered across the nation at this time, and remember your children spread throughout the world. Now we are in a historical era where we must spread a global front and fight for the world. We cannot look to anyone or rely on anyone, so we only look to you and rely on you, moving only toward the destination you are heading.

Following the path you take in a battlefield where we cannot feel joy is our comfort, receiving your commands gives us strength, and your protection is our pride. We have taken this as our pride and have walked the path of your will, the sorrowful path of return, until now. We are still walking this path. We wish to continue on this path tomorrow and for the rest of our lives, so we hope and desire that you lead, guard, and protect us at all times. 

Merciful Father, please come to us; compassionate Father, extend your loving hand; powerful Father, remove evil and establish us in a position to receive the victory of recreation and the grace of resurrection. Thus, may we be equipped with the ability to achieve the second liberation and be established as a proud heavenly army, as a group that lacks nothing in its posture.

During this day, with your abundant grace, we offer the fruits of victory from the past year as we enter this harvest season, returning the joy of the year to you. We ask that we become a group that can take responsibility for the concerns you have left behind, following the bonds of love.

Please protect the mobilization team standing on the front lines representing your children scattered across the world. They have set out with your calling, and although they move on the earth, they are the heavenly army, the pioneers of heaven, and the embodiments of hope that heaven can look upon. Therefore, they must be strong and courageous.

No matter how high the enemy forces surrounding us may rise, may we become your sons and daughters, boldly displaying the appearance of heavenly soldiers who affirm the authority of heaven and can subdue the enemy. We earnestly hope and desire that you allow us to be your soldiers.

Father, please protect Korea. You know well the conflicting situations of the North and South, so we earnestly hope and desire that you watch over the path this nation must take. Please have compassion on this pitiful nation that must take steps to push forward from a position isolated in Asia. All sides are blocked. Now, in this position where we can only look to heaven, allow us to become a nation that earnestly seeks your strength, authority, protection, and guidance more than any other nation.

Allow us to be a nation that relies on you and follows you rather than trusting in anyone else or depending on any country. To do this, someone must stand at the forefront, and when we think that the group at the forefront is the group of unification, we realize how grave our responsibility is.

Father, we know that without you, we cannot handle everything, so please guide our path. We are grateful for the grace you have given us to lead us this far. When we reach the last critical path or the final peak, we must run toward the suffocating slope without looking back, and when we face the final battle, we have the responsibility to surpass the peak until the end of our lives. Therefore, Father, we earnestly ask that you make us your children who can recognize our current position and prepare ourselves for the direction from which the enemy attacks.

Father, please be with the countless children who gather in your name, and allow us to fulfill our significant responsibilities as nations can embrace you. 

All these words I have offered in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We often make decisions based on comparisons, determining what is bigger or smaller, better or worse, or who is ahead or behind, based on relationships of before and after, left and right, and above and below. Or we may center on ourselves, saying someone is bigger or smaller or ahead of us. When making decisions in such positions, there is always someone who serves as the standard. That standard is always centered around oneself, meaning that one judges based on oneself. When I say, "I am good," that standard becomes me. When I say, "I am bad," I am also the standard.

What is the standard point that can solve all problems?
Today, we understand that humanity has fallen. When we think about the fact that humanity has fallen, that fallen position is diverse. When we look at ourselves as individuals, there are thousands of ancestors connected to us. Among them, there are those who are admirable and those who are not. There are those who are high and those who are low. There are those who stand in front and those who stand behind.

When we think this way, we cannot see that a thousand people stand on one path, in one position. If a thousand people are arranged in a line centered around one supreme good person, can we say that the ancestors stand in such an organized position? If a thousand people are centered around one point, we can say they are drawing a circle. However, they are not drawing a perfect circle; they are standing in their own ways. Therefore, we cannot help but imagine that all thousand people stand in different positions.

Even when we consider ourselves as individuals, the ancestors have gone through a process to connect with us, and today’s "me" is born as their descendant. When we ask whether I am worthy of the true standard that all these ancestors desire, I realize that I am standing at a slightly different angle.

When we consider whether there were ancestors who stood at the point of unity centered on the truth, we cannot say that there were. This has been the case not just for one year, but for thousands or even tens of thousands of years of history. The longer the history, the more distant it becomes, the less clear the standard becomes; it cannot become more certain, but rather must become increasingly ambiguous, and we cannot help but conclude that it becomes less perfect.

Generally, we are such beings; we are such individuals. From that perspective, when I say, "I am good. Oh, today was good," the question becomes what position that goodness stands in. Even when we consider a family, if we say, "Our family is happy right now," what kind of position does that happiness occupy? If there is a central point of true happiness, is it to the east, west, south, or north? Do we know where that position is? We do not know.

The same goes for a nation. When we say, "The Republic of Korea is unhappy. It is in a position to become unhappy," we must ask from which position it is unhappy. We do not know this. Also, when we look at the world, it is not developing into a higher world where humanity can add more hope; rather, it is a world that drives countless people who have sought higher ideals into a state of despair. When we face this global situation, the question becomes what position this world occupies centered around a true standard that can represent the historical hopes. This is not a simple question.

A person who can present the truth
When we consider ourselves as individuals living in such an environment, and also look at nations or humanity, the question of what standard we can hope for becomes an important one. Where is the standard I should follow as an individual? This cannot be resolved within the short timeframe in which I live today.

The standard that can resolve this is not within me. It is necessary to find some different standard, a more valuable content standard, and to establish a relative relationship with that standard. Only then can we truly find value and hope. However, if we are in a position where we cannot even think of this or find it, then boasting about today’s self is extremely foolish. We cannot help but think about this issue.

If there is a true human being, that true human will seek the path to represent history, saying, "Humanity, this is the true standard you must follow." If there is a true person, that person will cry out, teach, and pave the way until they find that path, even if it means enduring great sacrifices on behalf of humanity. If someone knows that path but insists on going alone, that person is not a true person.

Truth is not limited to individuals. It is applied beyond the whole and seeks to establish valuable connections beyond the whole. Truth is something that everyone likes and seeks, and therefore it must be present everywhere. For this reason, if there is someone who knows the true path on behalf of humanity, that person must fulfill their responsibility to ensure that valuable connections exist everywhere, even if it means making all kinds of sacrifices. This is the responsibility of a life that stands in the position of truth; one cannot stand in a position that says, "It is difficult, so as long as I know, that is enough."

From that perspective, if there is indeed such a true person among humanity, that person must live with a serious commitment centered on the truth. This is the issue. How seriously and meaningfully do they live? Furthermore, that person must recognize that the value of that truth is greater than any authority or power, and that it is more valuable than any purpose that people of that time may wish to fulfill. They must push through, reform, and pioneer that environment, bravely engaging in fierce struggles.

If one does not feel that value, they may not understand, but if someone knows, "This is the true truth. No one can oppose this truth. Only this can determine absolute victory, and only this can determine absolute perfection," then that person...
Even if one is in a lonely environment, rather than being pushed out by that environment, one must purify the environment and become the best standard figure within it. In other words, one must pioneer the relative environment as a subject. If one fails to pioneer the relative environment, one will ultimately perish. One will be confined to oneself.

A human life is limited, as it is a journey of less than a hundred years, and if one cannot pioneer this environment within that time, one will perish. Therefore, we must understand that we bear a historical mission to engage in all sorts of struggles to expand our second realm of rights by investing our lives.

Then, can all the people in that environment truly know that person? This is the issue. Can they recognize that "this is indeed the truth"? They do not all know. If they did, would they all be the same? Can individuals affirm, "Indeed, that person is true," and have that recognized by others? They cannot. They see but do not understand. They must see that the person has the same features and body, but we cannot know the value of that content. Therefore, no matter how much one asserts oneself, one cannot be acknowledged as the subject in that place.

When the heart, words, and actions become one, joy follows.

So what must be done? There needs to be a re-creation. Such people cannot form relationships with others as they are, so a movement of adaptation is necessary to ensure that they can understand. It is about saying, "Be like me." Through resemblance, more valuable connections are formed, and a more valuable standard of goodness is established. The question is, how should this be demonstrated?

People live centered on their words, actions, and minds. They live with their speech, behavior, and intentions. So how should this be demonstrated? It must be shown through words. We must teach the individual life view that "individuals should be like this." What kind of individual should one become? One must become an individual who can move a family. That is essential. The family must move this individual. That is the normal world.

Children born to husbands or wives from a world of goodness can learn and be good in such a world, but if they are in a world that lacks this, a true person representing that world must be developed. It must be created. Therefore, one must create one's own perfection. One must establish a realm of completion.

If one is a man, one must create this as a man and establish a completed family. (There is a brief period of silence in the recording.)

The wife should say, "What my husband says is truly good. I must give up everything of mine and accept my husband's words one hundred percent." It should be like this. Not only in words but also in actions, she must establish an internal connection that says, "If he goes east, I will go east too." Shouldn't it be like that?

The wife must go where the husband goes. Therefore, she must eliminate everything she used to say and become someone who embodies the content of what her husband says. Not only in words but also in saying, "Where he goes, I must go." Only then can they go together until the end. If he goes east and she says, "He can go east, but I feel bad, so I will go the other way," that is where the breakdown begins.

Therefore, if there is such a true husband, one must follow him in words and also act together. In acting, regardless of where one has been, one must act based on one direction. One must act centered on one direction. That is without question.

In speaking and acting, these must not conflict. Isn’t that right? If words differ, it is said, "That person's words and actions are different," right? At such times, evaluations are made based on those differences, and they are not good evaluations but rather negative ones. When words and actions differ, criticism arises from that difference. Although it may be vague, the heart serves as the standard for words and actions. Without being in a place where the heart is the center, that person cannot become the center. Isn’t that so? In a vague position, if the heart is the standard for words and actions, then words must become one based on that standard heart. After that, actions must become one. Only then can one become a person whose heart resembles and is united with the heart. Isn’t that right?

What does such a heart move around? It revolves around purposes, life views, movements for the nation, or movements for personal success, manifesting in various forms.

Where does the heart move? Does it move for personal purposes? Does it move for the purpose of the family? It varies accordingly. Does it move for the purpose of the nation? Or does it move for the purpose of the world? Furthermore, to borrow the terminology of the Unification Church, does it move for the sake of heaven? Ultimately, does it move for the sake of God's love? This is the question.

For your heart to emerge as a valuable existence that serves as the standard for words and actions, the heart, words, and actions must become one. Only when this is unified can one find joy based on the foundation of that heart in the current position. Is it like this? When the heart, words, and actions differ, one cannot be joyful. When that difference arises, one feels anxious, feels self-restricted, and is subject to constraints. We can feel this in our daily lives.

Joy comes only from relative relationships.

In light of this position, what must be present in a person's heart? One cannot have just a heart. What must be in that heart? Analyzing the valuable contents within the heart reveals knowledge (知), emotion (情), and will (意). When analyzing the heart, there are intellectual elements, volitional elements, and emotional elements.

Then, what does the heart seek to act upon? Ultimately, there is something that can serve as the standard of the heart. That is joy. It is for the sake of joy. Although it is not certain, it is based on joy. It does not base itself on sadness. Isn’t that right? Are there people who enjoy sadness in their hearts and bodies and in various environmental aspects? Everyone seeks joy as the standard and wishes to have that heart.

So what is true joy? What is truly joyful in the heart? To be more joyful, one can only find joy when the heart, actions, and words are completely united in facing a purpose. When the heart, words, and actions become one, one seeks to remain centered on joy, and the standard of that joy is emotion (情). It is the so-called heart (心情) spoken of in the Unification Church. In our Unification Church, we speak of heart (心情) rather than just the emotion (情) of knowledge, emotion, and will. There must be a central emotion that allows for joy in a place where the heart, words, and actions are united. In other words, there must be a standard emotion that serves as a basis. There must be valuable content that can lead to greater joy.

One cannot be joyful alone. Joy can only be found in relative relationships. Can one be joyful alone? If one is laughing alone, they are considered a mad person. If I were to speak diligently here alone without you, I would be considered a mad person. When I speak diligently, you must listen earnestly to that content and unite with those words, so that both you and I can be joyful. It is not for the sake of sadness that we speak. It is for the sake of joy.

When there is a space where one can say, "That was a great speech. I really enjoyed that," both the listener and the speaker feel joy. What joy does the speaker feel? When one speaks from the morning, they must sweat, and sweating is a form of self-consumption, so what joy is there in that? When one works hard and the value of that hard work is realized, then there is joy.

Why is there joy? There is no joy in suffering. Isn’t that right? There is absolutely no joy in suffering. Why is there joy? Because the standard of my heart and the standard of the other’s heart are in harmony. When one speaks centered on a purpose and affirms what has been said, complying with it to become one, another heart merges with that heart, resulting in two hearts.

What happens to the two? It is not that one becomes two; rather, two come together to become one. From one's perspective, it ultimately becomes, "I have gained one." "Whether I was the motivation or someone else was, we have both gained one more place, so it is not a loss, and therefore I am joyful." This is how it becomes.

Therefore, a person without a counterpart is a pitiful person. No matter how loud they shout, if there is no counterpart, that sound disappears. The more one invests, the more it gradually disappears. When there is a true counterpart whom I genuinely love, it seems that the more I invest, the more it disappears, but what happens? Although it seems to disappear, it emerges. When one sees that emergence, it becomes theirs, and they also become necessary to that person. It seems like a loss, but in the end, it becomes a plus. Where does this come from? It exists only where joy can be found. This is how it works.

An environment where one can be joyful cannot exist alone. Joy can only be found in the application of relative conditions. Why is there joy? Because the counterpart becomes a second self. When one adds to one, it emerges as a reproductive second self, and thus joy arises from being two.

What will happen when there are two? It is not just about being as they are; rather, two must become one. Everything is like this. The heart spoken of in our Unification Church is also relative. Where should the heart go? What is the path of the heart? It seeks to go the path of joy. To be joyful, what must happen? There must be a dynamic connection to a higher standard of joy.

Therefore, without emotional content, there can be no happiness, hope, or any kind of joy. Can there be? When one is joyful, one laughs. If one is joyful, one is already laughing, right? Why does one laugh? Who does one laugh at? Do they laugh alone? If one laughs alone, they are a mad person. When one laughs, is it for oneself? Do they look in a mirror and laugh? As one’s complexion changes and expressions change, who do they laugh for? Is it for oneself? It is a laughter that occurs because of the counterpart. Isn’t that right? When asked why one laughs, they say, "I laugh because I feel good." Why do they feel good? Is it because they are alone? No, it is because there is a counterpart.

Therefore, when there is a counterpart and two become one, laughter naturally arises. It must arise, and that is joy. The expression of joy comes not from oneself but from the counterpart.

A person who looks in the mirror and laughs every day is a lonely person. A lonely widow or widower is like that. Look at this, is it true or not? Before you get married, you look in the mirror a lot. You have probably experienced this. But after getting married, it becomes, "What is there to look in the mirror for?" Therefore, I hope your hearts are joyful.

Without passing through a heart-centered standard, one cannot enter the ideal world.

So what is the subject of the heart? That is emotion (情), but emotion is not just vague; it serves as the standard upon which we can feel joy in our hearts. This is referred to as the standard of heart (心情) in the Unification Church.

It must be that there is a heart within emotion. That heart does not exist arbitrarily. The standard of that heart does not exist arbitrarily. Among those standards, there is only one standard of personality. There are two emotions, the emotion of "heart" (心情) when we say "emotion." The standard of heart centered on the individual is one, and the standard of heart centered on the family is also one. Of course, the individual and family are two, but the standard of heart that can be established by combining these two is the absolute center of the universe among men and women.

The path of this heart is... Will it go straight or will it go in a winding way? Is there anyone who wants a winding path? It is undoubtedly a straight line. Therefore, the path that the family takes, the emotion between spouses, the positive emotion of the man and the negative emotion of the woman, must be combined and tied together, and there is only one path. Even if there are many families, there is only one.

Why is that? It is because we are destined to seek absolute joy. You are seeking absolute happiness, absolute hope, and absolute ideals, right? (Then, while writing, he explains.) If there is a starting point that can connect to that absolute purpose, can it be done arbitrarily? There must be a single path that connects the direction of this heart and that direction without conflict, and no matter how long the process is, it cannot change. Only then can it connect to the purpose of the absolute subject; otherwise, it is impossible.

Therefore, there is only one emotional standard that can lead to a couple. This is true for couples centered on the family, but when there are family members centered around the family, the emotional standard that the family members must follow, the standard tied to the couple, and the emotional standard that allows the family to move forward is one. Without passing through that path, one cannot enter the absolute ideal world. Such a thing must exist.

If it is a neighborhood, if the neighborhood loves each other and wants to become one, the neighborhood must unite. Also, to improve the North and South, must they become two? No, they must become one. What must be the standard for becoming one? Is it okay to say that this is good and that is good, and that up and down can be reversed? No, there must be a standard for becoming one. There must be a standard.

What is that standard? Whether it becomes the subject or the object, unless it determines the standard, there will be no way to become one. If each side insists on being the standard, conflict will continue. Isn’t that right? If two positives try to become one, they will repel each other. Do they become one? They are bound to repel each other. This happens day and night, even while sleeping. Enemies repel each other even in sleep.
It's a fight, isn't it? The more extreme the enemy, the more they fight even while sleeping, while eating, and even in the bathroom, which shouldn't be said. They fight 24 hours a day. Since they fight 24 hours a day, they fight all year round, twelve months a year. If they fight all year round, they are bound to fight for a lifetime. A person who fights like this throughout their life is always unhappy. They are not happy throughout their life.

So, those who seek revenge are all pitiful people. When you see that, Jesus said to love your enemies, and wow! If you see this, you realize that they are not foolish people. If it is the style of Pyongan Province, I should hit back. That enemy, while I was in prison… Everyone has a conscience. If someone has done something wrong, they feel guilty, and they must confess and resolve it. Right? That person who played a leading role in putting me in prison suddenly appeared.

He is a communist official. So, when he appeared, was I feeling good or bad? How do you think I felt when I saw that person? "You felt bad." I felt bad. I felt bad when I faced him. But even though I knew well, I pretended not to know. I said, "I do not know who you are." Why would I not know? I saw him every day, so I was just playing dumb. "I am so-and-so, and you do not know me?" So, I said, "Oh, is that so? I did not realize." When I looked into his eyes, they used to be fierce, but now they were softened, and he appeared looking somewhat human. He came to me, saying not to think badly of him for forgetting the past.

When he left, he bought me something to eat. But the question was whether to eat it or not. Should I eat it or not? It might be poisoned. Do you know if it is poisoned? What do you think I should do? "You should eat it." Why should I eat it? "Because you resolved your feelings." (Laughter) Did that person resolve his feelings, or did I? If I do not resolve my feelings, I should not eat it. If I resolve my feelings, then I can eat it with the joy of being more liberated than that person, and that is my victory.

The question was whether to accept the food and eat it or not. In a place like prison, food is very precious. You may not know, but when the first army was formed in Korea, young men would shout "Food! Food!" from the day they entered, but that is nothing. In prison…
If someone hears about food, they might snatch it away from each other, but the question is whether to eat it or not. It was serious. There was a time when I received it at lunch and didn't eat it until dinner, thinking seriously about it.  
What would God have done in such a situation? God is a God of love. Right? When the prodigal son was unfilial to his parents, betrayed his brother, and left home, if he returned with a tearful heart, bringing even his father’s clothes or a cane, would the father accept it or not? What do you think? Without love, there is no way to accept it. You cannot accept it without discovering the principle of love.  
When the prodigal son returns, repenting of all his past, shedding tears for his parents, and bringing something as a sign of love, that can, in turn, become a manifestation of the parents' love. This is how it works.  
Thinking seriously about that reminds me of sharing food with my family. Then I thought, if I were in that situation, would I have had the courage to visit? If I were to ask whether I could visit even to the prison, I cannot readily answer that I could do so. This is something to think about. Isn't that right? You would face various complicated issues, such as how to treat that person.  
When he came to the prison, he must have prepared himself to be rejected, humiliated, and to lose face. Moreover, he was a communist party official. Although they call it a security team, he must have thought about the shame he would face in front of the guards. If he were to be spat on or slapped, wouldn’t he feel ashamed? He came disregarding his face and dignity. How much pain of conscience did he endure to disregard that? When I think about such things, I have seriously considered that he is still a person with potential. Because I thought that way, even after living my life, I still cannot forget that person. In prison life, even though he is an enemy, he remains someone I always think about. It is not a place of cursing. Still, I cannot shake the thought that such a person has loyalty and potential.  
How lonely is a place like prison? While considering one’s own dignity, there is a sense of responsibility to help someone in that lonely place, even if it’s just to share a meal. When I think that this person is feeling guilty because of me and has a desire to care for me under any conditions, that person becomes someone I can fully understand and remember in my heart. (There was a moment when the recording was not on.) Even though we are enemies, when someone leaves an emotional connection, there is a possibility to meet again in history and to live again. I am still thinking about this.  
How many times must you have felt lonely in that prison, Teacher? I can never forget the times you came to comfort me when I was in a lonely place. I can forget when relatives or others came, but I cannot forget those who formed such a bond of love. Do you understand what I mean? This shows that not all enemies are bad. I have felt that education can happen through such situations, and there is much to learn. Do you understand? “Yes.”  
If I think about this, among the Unification Church members, how grateful would someone be if they were in the military or in prison and someone visited them, whether as a family member or in some other relationship? Even if there are many family members, if there is even one person who visits, that person becomes a true friend. That person is certainly busy as well. Taking time out of their busy schedule to visit someone in that lonely place is not the usual sincerity of a person. I remember that person more than I do when a relative comes. You all need to think about this.  
Visiting and sympathizing with someone in a difficult situation becomes a great opportunity to form a close bond. So, if someone among your family goes to the military or to prison, of course, the teacher should visit them, but even if you cannot go, you should leave such a legacy and walk the path of such connections. If you do so, you can leave a standard of education that says you should do good for the other person throughout your life. A person who has had such an experience, even when they are about to die, will leave a will saying, “Be like that person.”  
I feel that such connections must be preserved among the members of our Unification Church. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” Visiting someone when they are lonely is the quickest way to receive forgiveness if one is in a position to be forgiven, and it also becomes a condition to be remembered deeply among friends. I wanted to remind you to remember this.
