**The Warrior of Unification**  
Everyone should experience prison for about a year and a half. Why? Because there is so much to learn in prison.  
Why is there so much to learn? A learned person among people knows the value of every issue. For the Republic of Korea, they understand its value better than someone who has not learned or does not know something. The more you learn, the more you understand, right?  
You can feel a higher value in prison.  
Even if you say, “Let’s love our country,” if you have a lot of experience and knowledge, or if you know through history or through patriots until now, you will naturally come to know the value of the Republic of Korea. Isn’t that so?  
Someone who says, “I must become a capable person,” must study. Why do you study? Because you know the value of that field. This is how it works.  
So, what kind of place is prison? Why is it necessary? It is a place where you can learn more than anywhere else. First, you learn about what you wear. “Wow, clothes are really precious!” Do you understand? It is a place where you can truly understand the value of clothing.  
When you enter a cell, it is not a heated room. It is not a place where steam comes in, and while burning coal, there are people who die from coal gas, but it is a place that has nothing to do with warmth. In places like Hungnam, the average temperature in winter is between minus 18 and 21 degrees. Because it is such a cold place, it does not matter whether you block the walls or have some windbreak; everything is connected. Do you understand? So, it is the same whether inside or outside. The inside of the prison and the outside are the same. You know that, right?  
Rather, in winter, the prison is colder. Why? Because the outside is warmed by the sun, if you go out and sit in a sunny spot, it is warm, but the prison…
There is no such place. Just because the sun comes out, you can't stick your head out and say, "Oh, let's bask in the sun." This prison is a place that is cold during the day and cold at night. 

That's why, in that situation, what silk clothes? The thought of silk clothes is completely out of the question; they have nothing to do with it at all. It is a place where quantity is more important than quality, even more than silk clothes. Do you understand what I mean? Even a burlap sack would be good. A thick burlap sack is better... You know that feeling, right? It's something that only those who have experienced it directly can understand, no matter how much I explain it.

When it comes to needing silk clothes or needing a burlap sack, people living in prison do not need fancy clothes like silk or satin. They throw all that away and fight to grab a thick burlap sack first. That's what prison is. Therefore, it is a place that understands the value of clothing better than anyone else. Do you get that? Do you understand? "Yes."

When you see that kind of value, sitting there with a thick burlap sack on, if it feels a bit warm, you think, "How happy I am...." Do you know what I mean? (laughs) "Even though I am wearing a burlap sack, today is better than anyone else. How happy I am at this moment!" That is a place where you can praise the value of living. It doesn't have to be a burlap sack; even a sack made of straw would be fine. If you are shivering and can put on a straw sack to keep warm, you can smile even while being inside it. Do you understand? If that happens, it becomes a paradise.

So, the prison is a place where you can feel a higher value than anything else. It is a place where you can learn things that you cannot learn anywhere else in the world. For young people, it is the best place. Do you understand? Just because I say this, it doesn't mean that "the teacher said that because he spent about a year and a half in prison, there is a lot to learn in prison, but no matter how much I go, if I believe in the Unification Church, there is no way to go to prison, so I should commit a theft and go to prison once." That won't do. (laughter) That's an exception.

So, when you go to prison, everything has value. Where can you truly understand the value of clothing? In prison, in prison.

Also, the eyes are for seeing. But nowadays, people in the world dislike seeing others. The world has become that way. When you go out to Myeongdong, there are all sorts of people. How many people are there? When you are walking and someone recognizes you and says, "Hey, you and I have a connection. I feel like I've seen you before," your heart sinks. "Oh my, why is that person acting like that?" You can be surprised just by seeing someone. However, in prison, people are like that. Do you understand? When a person appears before you, whether they are good or bad, handsome or ugly, beautiful or plain, regardless of gender or age, if someone comes to visit you, their eyes sparkle like lightning. Do you understand? Since there is no way to express the exciting feeling, that is how they show it. So, you cannot imagine how much they miss people. If there is someone related to you, you are very grateful. There can be nothing more grateful than that. It doesn't matter whether the person who appears is good or bad. You cannot be more grateful to someone who comes to find you. Even if there is a Republic of Korea, there is no place other than prison where you can recognize and treat the value of that one person even more than the Republic of Korea itself. Do you understand?

Even when you hear a voice or listen to words, what is the best word in the world? For someone who has been in prison for a while, hearing that they will be released is a word that makes their ears perk up. Do you understand? I am about to go out well, and liberation is happening... Then the world... That is something indescribable. You would sit up straight even if you were sleeping.

Prison is a place where you can learn things that you cannot learn in the world.

Now, everyone, because North and South Korea are not unified, there is a lot of fuss about negotiations and Red Cross talks, right? But wouldn’t it be wonderful if North and South Korea were liberated? But is there anyone who hears that and feels like they can't live without jumping for joy? No. Even the most patriotic person would not think, "Oh, hearing that is better than dying!" There aren't many people who think that way. Is that right? No, it is not.

However, in prison, hearing "We are going to be released. We are going to be liberated." is a more welcome word than dancing and celebrating in a church. Do you understand? The ears that hear, the eyes that see...

Next, there is the sense of smell. When you are in prison, your nose becomes incredibly sensitive. If there is a neighborhood in the south, when the southern wind blows and passes by you, you can tell, "Ah, they are cooking soup over there." You can know this without anyone telling you. How sensitive it is! You can tell when they are slaughtering a cow and cooking beef soup within ten miles. You can understand the value of smelling 100 percent... You cannot know that value outside of prison. That is why this nose is also a place where you can receive specialized training! Do you understand? So, prison is not bad? "No!" It is not! (laughs)

Should I continue? Next, this mouth, it is meant to speak and to eat. When you meet someone you are happy to see, you whisper and talk, right? And when you see something delicious, you eat it well, right?

You don't know how much you miss being able to whisper. Those who have not experienced it will not understand no matter how much I explain, so it is better not to explain at all. Just look at the expressions and remember. You cannot imagine how happy it would be to have that time to whisper... If I had that time, "How happy would I be? How joyful would I be?" You cannot imagine that longing in your heart.

That is why the place where you can recognize and appreciate the value of forming connections through your mouth is only in prison. Do you understand? "Yes." There is no place that teaches such values better than prison, so what is prison? It is the best place. (laughs)

Next, this mouth also does what? It eats. I first realized how delicious rice is. The only place where you can truly understand how precious rice is... Even if you live a thousand years in the world, you may not know the taste of rice, but when you go to prison, you can truly understand how precious rice is. The only place where you can learn the value of rice that you cannot learn in the world is prison, so that is why prison is the best. (laughs)

What kind of place is prison? It is a place where a stick goes back and forth. In the old days, during the Japanese occupation, a club would go back and forth. When I went to the North and was interrogated, when I was tortured... This kind of talk is inappropriate in front of women. Ladies, cover your ears. (laughs) I said to cover your ears, but if you don't and then criticize someone for saying such things, you become worse than me. Ladies, cover your ears. But if you want to listen, go ahead. This is not good talk. Men know all about it... (laughs)

Everyone, do you know about the reproductive organs of a bull? They are this long, and if you dry them, there is no stick as magnificent as that among sticks. There might be people who have heard that when someone goes to prison, they get hit with some kind of stick. I wondered what it looked like, and after going in and being tortured, I said, "Hey, I don't know the name of that thing you are holding, but let's find out what kind of wood it is before you hit me." So I learned what it was. After knowing and getting hit, I asked for it, and it was swaying, and it looked magnificently shaped. When you hit it once, it makes a sound. Do you understand? That is why the only place where you can truly know the taste of being beaten is prison.

Why? Because getting hit by your mother or father is because you did something wrong, but here, even if you didn't do anything wrong, you get hit as if you did. Even someone who did well can be hit as if they did something wrong, and that is why they end up wetting themselves while saying they did something wrong. So, it is the most severe beating. A man who boldly goes out with his convictions even while being beaten deserves to be praised.

Through the beating... The beating truly determines the value of a wonderful person. Among the beatings, the most severe beating, once you get hit, you may not understand it in words, but your stomach goes up and down, up and down. Do you understand?

When I was in prison during the Japanese occupation, it was a time when they were trying to behead the Japanese emperor, so I was tortured in prison, and the hardest thing was... Try it once. Put a wooden stick here... During the Japanese occupation, there were leather shoes worn by the military. They were shoes with nails that made a clattering sound. You cannot know that unless you have experienced it. Do you understand?

Even so, I said, "Hit me, you bastard! Who loves the Republic of Korea more, my patriotism or your patriotism for Japan? You and I are enemies." And I fought magnificently.

So, what was the taste of the beating? Even if you get beaten severely, you feel, "Because I did this, I will repay it tenfold." Where else can you receive such education about beatings? "In prison." Only in prison! That is why prison is good. (laughs)

Prison is the place where you can be closest to nature.

Should I continue? When you wake up in the morning and open your eyes, you see the morning glow. Whether it is black, yellow, or red, they are all good. Everything is filled with hope. "Wow, looking at that from a free perspective, accepting it with all my strength, today is a wonderful day." You have that time to praise it and can immerse yourself in dreams and reflections. Then, when the morning sunlight shines, you are completely captivated.

What is sunlight? It is like a thread of taffy, or honey, or whatever good expression you want to use. "Oh, this is wonderful!" The rays of sunlight feel like they are all there for you. There is no place to learn better than looking at sunlight through a window! Do you understand?

So, the person who truly appreciates the sun is in prison! Why? Because the person who can love the sun the most is in prison. Prison is a place where you can praise the sun, so it is not bad! That is what I mean.

Also, I caught flies in prison and played with them every day. (laughs) Friends in prison are not the guards; they are these, right? (laughs) They call them the "wild boar brigade." Because they crawl around, they are called that. If you stay in prison for a long time... There is a place where the clothes are stitched. You don't even need to catch them. If you say you will catch two, two come out. (laughs) When I talk about this, I don't know if it will make you feel bad, but it is not bad.

If I write a book about this, prison might become famous. I don't intend to write a book, but since it is not bad, I share it. I catch a fly and place it on my palm, saying, "I caught one. I caught two. I caught three." (laughs) I can catch ten at once. When I talk about this, people say, "Oh, doing all sorts of things in prison..." In fact, I did all sorts of things. Doing this makes you warm. Do you understand? In winter, there are many bugs in prison. If you catch one and put it in a warm place, since the room is cold, they all gather there. That is how it is. Try it and see. (laughs) Why? Because it is physiological. They try to crawl in. If you catch ten, then they will try to huddle together to stay warm. "Ah, this won't do." So if you catch ten, twenty, thirty, fifty, they will form a circle. When you roll them, if one falls out, they will try to crawl back in. That is a lot of fun... That is why in prison, bugs are not enemies but friends! (laughs)

No one in the world likes bugs. But if you can sing and discuss with bugs and play with them, if you can have that kind of education, it is the best education. The only place you can receive that education is in prison, so prison is not bad!

Now, in summer, the flies come buzzing in. "Hey, you are better than me!" They come right in front of me and rub their hands together. That makes me feel bad. "Hey, what are you bragging about by rubbing your hands in front of me?" If I blow at them, they fly away and then come back. "Oh, this one won't do." So I think, "This time, if I rub my legs, I will catch it, and if I don't, I won't." Sure enough, it comes right back and blinks its eyes. Flies don't blink, but it is doing that. "I will definitely catch this one." So I talk to myself and get excited, thinking, "Hey, should I let it go?" and then I catch it... Catching one fly in that serious place is more joyful than catching a bull. (laughs) Do you understand what I mean? Then if it flies away, I think, "Oh no, that feels bad. Today must be unlucky." There is no place other than prison where you can play like that.

Thinking about catching it, I try to catch it as it flies away, and I cannot let it go! If I let it go, it will be a big deal. I catch it and say, "You are caught now. This is revenge." It is not just about forgiveness; it is about revenge. "Hey, this will hurt, but bear with it; I will make it not hurt." I hit it and pull it out. If you hold its body tightly, its butt stretches out. Try it. You can pull off its wings too. Even if we think about it, it seems like it wouldn't hurt. If you ask if it hurts, it seems to say it doesn't hurt. (laughs) Since I pulled off one side, if I say, "Bear with it," and pull off the other side, even though the place where the wings were pulled off might hurt, if I let it go, it will still run around well. (laughs)

Then I gather tissues in the shape of a wall and make a fence, and I race them. Whoever completes a lap first can leave through a small hole. If I leave a little hole, they will try to go out. They will run around. If I catch three and say, "Whoever is first, second, big one, small one," it becomes really fun. (laughs)

I could go on forever talking about this. Even one fly becomes an object of longing. "Hey, if you could talk, I would send my wishes to my hometown..." It could fly all the way to my hometown. "It might bring back news..." A single fly can become a friend. Everyone hates flies, but among friends, it can be a friend, a subject of discussion. There is no place other than prison where you can receive such education. That is why prison is not bad. That is how it is.
If we keep talking like this, there will be no end. It's been a long time now, so let's stop. There are plenty of such stories. Depending on the season, when it snows, one becomes very sentimental. "The beggar who came last year has come again this year..." Like that song, "The snow that fell last year is falling again this year; I thought I wouldn't see snow in the prison, but here it is again." In such moments, one can reflect on the past. "Ah! What have I done for a year?" Based on the changes in nature, one can reflect on their entire life. "I was born here, my parents loved me like this and that, I went to school like this and that, and now I've ended up living in a prison, facing winter and the snow falling all around me. After this season passes, spring will come, summer will come, autumn will come, and winter will come again, bringing this snow, but I hope I won't be here next winter..." While thinking about the future, one can seek personal development and new hope, and there is no place other than prison for that.

That's why, if I were a young person, I would say that at least a year and a half of official prison education should be provided. If I become the Minister of Education or have the power to govern the country, I would like to try it out. It's really true.

There is nothing unnecessary and nothing needed in prison.

What was the happiest thing for me in prison? Shall I tell you? I won't, because it seems too petty. 

It's fun to talk, and it doesn't take much time, but I want to do it, but I'm too embarrassed to! (laughter) Even if I'm embarrassed, if you want to hear it, since I'm someone who has decided to live like this, if you really want to hear it, let's give it a try. Do you want to hear it? "Yes." Don't laugh. Alright, let's give it a try.

If a man's dignity is like this, he doesn't belong to the smaller group among the people of the Republic of Korea. I weighed 97 kilograms, but recently I did some fasting exercises and lost 10 kilograms, bringing me down to 87 kilograms. Don't worry about the fat people, the chubby people. If you fast, you will quickly become slim. Do you understand? Members of the Unification Church, if they want to become fat after a week of fasting, just drink water; if they want to slim down, they just need to stop drinking water and eating. So, there's nothing to worry about.

Now, look. In prison, there is nothing unnecessary, and there is nothing needed. What does that mean? "There is nothing unnecessary, and there is nothing needed." That’s what it means. When you go to prison, even if you have a lot of wealth, it becomes unnecessary. Do you need household items? Do you need a radio? Do you need a television? Having those will only cause trouble. Even though they are all necessary, they are unnecessary in prison. Do you understand?

Then, if there is nothing unnecessary, what is needed? What is the most necessary thing? The most necessary thing is a toilet! (laughter) This is the most unpleasant and petty thing. "What is that needed for? The most necessary thing in the world is unnecessary, and what is necessary is a toilet?" You might think that, but isn't it necessary? "It is necessary."

Let me tell you a story; since I've brought up the topic of toilets, let's talk about it. "As evening approaches, my butt hurts and I'm bored, and the teacher appears again, wondering what to do? It’s unpleasant to have the same medicine again, but it can be reused." But reusing it can be beneficial. So, look.

As you know, in Hungnam Prison, the front is by the sea. It gets really cold there. Because the wind is strong, pebbles fly in. It’s really cold. So, for the people living in prison... Do you think the owners of the prison would treat their guests well? It doesn't work that way. Right? What they give is only the leftovers, even from the radish greens, and they give the rest. That's how it is. Just because winter has come, the season for catching pollack, they won't serve pollack soup. Do you understand?

What is needed in the world is not needed in prison.

But there comes a time when you can eat meat to your heart's content. Isn’t that good news? When they bring fish in a basket and say, "Hurry and eat," and open the door to shove it in, how wonderful would that be? When is that? The sea in front of Hungnam is a place where mackerel is caught in abundance. Once they are caught, they come in heaps. Then, they all become fertilizer. Mackerel is quite oily. Eating raw mackerel is delicious. If you eat one that has been sitting for a few days, it’s not good, but if you eat one that is still alive, it’s really tasty. During the mackerel season, it’s the cheapest, cheaper than radish greens, and cheaper than anything else, so they bring in a truck and say, "Hey! You want to eat? Eat to your heart's content." They bring in a whole truck, steam it in a large pot, and fill a basket to the brim. "Here, eat as much as you want." But after starving for a year, your intestines have become thin, and all the fat has disappeared, so can you digest the oil? It’s certain that you can’t. Since you can’t digest it, it just passes through. (laughter) There are no traffic accidents here. Do you understand? (laughter) After eating dinner, you have to sleep for just one night and then go to work, but you can’t go to work after going to the toilet, right? In the morning, everyone... You can’t wake up early. If you wake up at that time, you’ll be accused of conspiracy to escape. So, you have to wait together. When the time comes and everyone shouts "Go out!" dozens of people have been sitting all night, and even though there are still many successors and reapplicants, when they shout "Go out!" what can you do? You can’t all get out at once, so you shuffle out slowly. When that happens, it’s truly an exhibition. Do you understand? (laughter)

Listening to someone who has actually experienced this is what makes it interesting. Isn’t it? It’s fun, right? Even though it’s unfortunate, it’s fun. Listening to someone else’s words isn’t interesting. It feels unpleasant. But when someone who has actually experienced it speaks, it’s full of fun.

Since you are absolutely not allowed to have anything like metal, just in case, if you wake up at five and get inspected until eight... In summer, sitting for three hours, what do you think will happen? You’ll see everything. (laughter) "Here... Oh!" while maintaining some dignity... Then, while sitting, if some unpleasant water collects, and someone can’t hold it in, it rises up. (laughter) This is the kind of bizarre situation that unfolds. There may be one or two people who criticize it, but "You do it, I do it," everyone is the same... (laughter) So laugh! Laugh! Laugh freely. That’s how it is. Whether it’s me or you, we are all the same, so is there anything to criticize? That’s how the saying came about. "When spring comes back, you have to do it once." What does that mean? It means you have to go to the toilet. (laughter) So, a slogan was born: "Those who can’t go to the toilet are fools." (laughter)

No matter how much you travel the world... There’s no place where you can learn such things other than prison.

People who have some dignity or prestige will hold it in until eight, and then finally "plop plop" at the end... (laughter) Even though it’s not cold, they have to come out early in the morning, so some people end up throwing up. This is not a lie; it’s a fact. When they shout "Go out!" all kinds of bizarre situations unfold beside you.

When that happens, those who can’t go will avoid those who can, and those who can will avoid those who can’t... Isn’t that how it is? But when they go out, over a thousand people hold hands in groups of four and line up. So they look for each other. This is like at a closing event, where someone loses their precious item and frantically searches for it. Such sights can only be seen in prison.

Even those who were dirty with each other will eventually hold hands tightly. Is there any way to avoid it? After three or four hours, it’s all done. While walking that ten-mile road, as they shuffle along, digestion happens, and their stomachs start making noises, "gurgle bang gurgle bang," creating a commotion. Those who were trying to maintain their dignity and were holding hands with those who couldn’t go will also end up saying, "Oh, wow, wow, wow!" (laughter)

When such scenes unfold, since everyone is the same, what is there to be embarrassed about? "If someone is laughing, you should also experience it; how busy and urgent it is. Those who haven’t experienced it don’t know." That’s what they say. I don’t know that content because I haven’t experienced it. Those who haven’t experienced it don’t know, so what can you do? There’s no excuse. This is the kind of bizarre situation that unfolds.

If you see this, the situation is unimaginable. That’s why when it’s mackerel season, while mackerel is appreciated, it also means that they have lost all semblance of humanity. I didn’t intend to talk about this. When I say I’m petty, this isn’t what I mean. This was just a seasoning for the conversation, and now let’s start talking.

When I say there is nothing unnecessary and nothing needed, it means that what is needed in the world is not needed there, and what is not needed in the world is needed there. Do you understand?

Then, what is not needed in the world? Is there anyone who likes needles? Is there anyone who likes syringes? Women do sewing, but they don’t really like needles. Why? Because when sewing, if they accidentally poke their fingernail, it’s only the needle that does it. Therefore, while a needle is necessary for sewing, women live with needles but don’t really like them.

One of the most precious things in prison is a needle.

Why am I telling you this? Just wait and see. How much does a needle cost? 1 jeon? "2 won." 2 won? That’s gone up a lot. But you shouldn’t dismiss that 2 won; it’s only a fifth of 10 won. So, it’s not that significant. In prison, they don’t give out needles. Every day, when handling urea ammonia, even if you wear cotton clothes, no matter how new they are, they won’t last three days. Woolen clothes last longer because they are resistant to acid, but cotton, no matter how new it is, will tear if you pull it after just three days. No matter how new the clothes are, they won’t last a week or two. So, you have to mend them every day.

Now, do they distribute needles in prison? Absolutely not. So, what do you do? You solve it yourself. If your butt is showing, it’s not good for your dignity. It would be fine to walk around with your butt hanging out, but if you tried to incite a strike in prison to get everyone to work naked, that would create problems, so that won’t work. You can’t just walk around with your butt hanging out, so you have to patch up the clothes. But if you want to mend them and don’t have a needle, what do you do? It’s a big problem.

So, what do you do? Do you know chopsticks? You grind the chopsticks on cement. You sharpen the chopsticks to use them. If you just stick it in, it will break. When you put in a stitch, there’s no way to poke it in hard. You have to wiggle it gently, as if dancing, saying, "You move aside, you move aside," and when the hole is made, then you apply saliva and twist the thread. It has to be twisted; it can’t just be straight. You twist the thread... Once it tears, it frays every day, and there’s no way to mend it. Even if you stay up all night, sometimes you just do a little bit and say, "Ah, I don’t know!" and with God’s help, you barely manage to mend it. That’s why you can’t imagine how much you long for a needle.

Now, women, don’t you know the value of a needle? So, reluctantly, someone like a teacher has to think. "I’ll make a needle." So, when you go to the factory, there are rails. These rails are made of steel. Then there’s wire. With this, "Let’s make a needle." You grind it on the cement floor. There’s wire that is as thick as a needle. This wire is sharpened to tie up sacks... The teacher is also skilled at tying sacks. There’s a metal hook for tying, and that’s steel too. The rail is like this (gesturing), it’s shaped like this. The wire is placed at the bend of the rail, and when you hit it with metal, it flattens. Do you understand? If you hit it too hard, it will break... So, you have to hit it just right. You have to hit it until it reaches the best standard where it won’t break. It can’t be done with just one attempt; it has to be done by someone with a lot of experience. Once it’s flattened, you have to bend it, but if you just bend it, it will break. So, it has to be bent into a circular shape.

If necessary, you break glass. Even if you get hit or scolded, pretending to put in a hook, if you throw it at an angle, something from above the factory might fall. There are no glass shards there. This glass is like a knife. That glass is quite hard. With that, you shave and make chopsticks. I’m the teacher there. That’s how you manage to survive.

You bend the wire and slowly, slowly, with that glass, you wear it down. When the hole finally forms, "Oh!" you can’t imagine that feeling. You don’t know the feeling when the hole is about to be made. If the hole is made, just hitting it will break it. After that, you bend it the other way and do the same on that side. With that, you make another needle-like object, and what do you hit it with? When the metal goes in, it gets stuck, right? Once it gets stuck, then you hit it from the other side. After that, you cut off the rest, and it becomes a needle. This needle is really nice. This needle is bigger and more useful than the ones made in society. Do you understand?

Then, it becomes an excellent needle. But it turns out that there’s no time to make even one needle. Where can you make it? Isn’t that right? So, once you make one, you can rent it out. "To borrow a needle, it costs a bag of flour." (laughter) Does that have value or not? It may seem petty and insignificant, but it’s a wonderful and exciting game, isn’t it? 

That doesn’t mean I sold flour.

So, I made some needles, gave some away, and used some, but the ones I made rusted, and since they were steel, they didn’t feel good. But if someone in prison has a real needle, everyone will know within two or three days. "There’s a real needle in some cell, a real needle." (laughter) If someone has a real needle in prison, they become famous.

That’s why you can’t imagine how precious a needle is. Do you understand? Women should think about that and know how to value even a single needle. At that time, it’s more precious than a husband. That’s how it is.

An unforgettable incident related to a needle.

But what happened was something I can’t forget.
I went out to the factory, and it was around two in the afternoon. I still remember the time. 
When I went to the factory and brought the sacks... the hardest part there is, 
when you have to fill 40 kilograms of ammonium sulfate, the hardest part is 
putting it into the sack and placing it on the scale. So who wants to do the hardest work? 
Starving and hungry, everyone tries to avoid the hard work, so inevitably, that job ends up being assigned to everyone, and I do it every day. If ten people are responsible for the work, that means 1,300 sacks. 
Bringing 1,300 sacks, filling them with fertilizer, pulling them out, tying them up, and finishing it all is the responsibility of one person for 130 sacks. If you get young people to do it, they will collapse. When you do 130, it feels like a small house. If you collapse, you might as well be dead. If you don’t want to die, you have to do it. You have to keep doing it until you die.

So while doing this work, oh, you see this thread, right? When the thread is visible... Generally, since the sacks are woven in the countryside, if there is thread, there is a needle attached. There is absolutely no needle left behind. Do you understand? If the thread is visible, it has become common knowledge that you will definitely find a needle. So when there is thread on the sack, anyone goes and tries to pull it out. I learned this there too, so even if you are a teacher of the Unification Church, you can’t do anything about it. Since the thread is visible, I thought maybe there was a needle, and sure enough, there was a needle. (Laughter) 

So I found the needle once. If you advertise that, it would be a big deal. So I said I was going to the restroom, and the joy of holding that needle at that time is something I wouldn’t trade for the world. When I think about it, how petty is that? Isn’t it petty? “Wow, even Teacher Moon of the Unification Church went to such lengths for a needle…” The needle is the king, and I stood in a position worse than a servant. This has remained as an unforgettable theme from my time in prison. When I see a needle at home, I can’t forget that moment. Do you understand?

Recreating and reevaluating people in prison
Also, when we eat, we always start with soup, right? When we eat, they always bring the soup first. One person brings the soup here, and another brings the rice over there, switching them like that. One day they switch it this way, and another day they switch it that way. Since one comes from the end and the other comes from this side, what we receive every day is either rice or soup. However, there is nothing more unpleasant than eating rice first and then drinking the soup. Try it. Eating rice and then drinking the soup feels really unpleasant. You have to eat the soup first and then have the rice; otherwise, you don’t feel like eating the rice, even if you receive it first. Therefore, you must eat the soup first. That soup is also salty. There are sayings like “the water across the pig river.” (Laughter) Why are you laughing? Is there something on my face? (Laughter)

When you eat the soup, sometimes it is so salty! When they cook soup in prison, do they think, “Since my husband or children eat like this, I should adjust the seasoning”? No, they just dump in a few buckets of salt. Whether it’s a lot or a little, they pour it in. If it all gets burnt, it becomes too salty to eat. Still, even if it’s salty, would you eat this precious soup, or would you throw it away? Would you throw it away? I don’t want to throw away that soup, even if it means dying. That bowl of thin soup is so precious...

Is there any prize for that? What prize? The prize is the hand. You have to support it with your hand... Eating it seriously, like a marksman aiming at a target. That’s how it is. The thought of eating a bowl of soup that is worth more than the world...

Also, when you look at the rice, it is barley rice that they give you. This rice is golden. In prison, soybean rice is the best. After that, mixed grain rice is even better. During holidays, like the first day of the lunar new year or the first day of May, there are holidays observed in the North, and on those days, they must give you golden rice. You receive it, but when you eat it after not having eaten it for a while, there is nothing more disappointing. Once it goes into your mouth, it already goes down. (Laughter) Even after eating, it feels like you haven’t eaten.

So everyone complains and suggests, saying, “On holidays, give us soybean rice.” Soybean rice is still good because it has a nice texture and is oily, so it has a stickiness when you eat it. Golden rice just goes down easily. So, the most disliked day is the holiday. I’m hungry. The taste of eating plain rice with your hands... I used to eat plain rice well before, but I learned how delicious plain rice is in prison. Do you understand? Side dishes are not the problem. It’s not about the side dishes; if a person eats deliciously, they will live. Complaining about beef side dishes or whatever is just the talk of the full. If you eat deliciously, you won’t gain weight. Do you understand what I’m saying? It’s still the same now. Because of that experience, it’s still like that.

The period from December 14 to December 23 is something I still can’t forget. It’s the period that left the most impression from my time in prison. Why is that period memorable? Because they served buckwheat noodles. You know buckwheat, right? The buckwheat used to make noodles. This noodle looks like this side and that side, and that side looks like this side. When they grind it, there are big and small grains, so when you peel off the skin, it passes through. Do you understand? They fill the quota and distribute it, so the big ones have their skins peeled off, and the small ones... the small ones are firmer. They boil it without peeling it, and when you eat it, it swells up. If you eat kimchi or something, it mixes well, but if you only eat buckwheat rice, it swells up. Try it.

Also, because they gave you the ones with skins, it takes more than an hour to eat them. But you have to eat the rice within 15 minutes. You can’t waste the rice, and you have to eat it, so I started thinking about how to eat the rice. Eating that rice and having indigestion leading to diarrhea was the most unforgettable pain of my time in prison.

That’s why when I think about eating buckwheat rice there, even now, when I receive a meal, I think, “Didn’t it used to be like this? Can I complain about not having side dishes? I should be grateful for this.” Even if I skip a meal for dinner, I think, “In the morning, I can compensate for not having dinner, can’t I? Even if I don’t eat dinner, I can’t complain.” This is how it goes. Unification Church members have fasted for a week, so they shouldn’t complain about food.

That’s why a place like prison is precious in terms of all these problems, and you should know that what is not precious is precious, and what is precious is not precious. In that sense, prison is the only place where you can recreate and reevaluate people. You can’t do that anywhere else. So prison is not bad. Therefore, I believe that if we put young people in there for official training, we can raise people who can unify the world. How does that sound? Is it good or bad? (Laughter) Answer me. Is it good or bad? “It’s good.” Those who say it’s good have received good education, while those who remain silent have received poor education.

Even if you don’t go to prison, you should at least undergo some form of training that resembles the experience of being in prison. That’s the educational method and training method of the Unification Church. Is it a good thing or a bad thing? “It’s good.” Is that really so? “Yes.” When you go to the neighborhood, even if you’re not eating well, you should think, “Hmm! We live the best.” That’s the style. When you go to the neighborhood and see people starving while they boast loudly, that’s the Unification Church style. Do you understand? If you see someone who has gone three or four meals without food, their face looks like they could run away thirty miles if someone saw them, yet... even if they’ve gone three or four meals without food, if their face is peaceful and smiling, filled with hope, that’s a Unification Church girl. How does that sound? Is it good or bad? “It’s good.” If that’s really the case, the man who marries that girl cannot be unhappy; that’s how it is.

That’s why when you go to the neighborhood, the young men perk up their ears and try to engage with the Unification Church girls. Isn’t that right? “……” Isn’t that right? You have to answer for it to be fun to talk. When evening comes and hunger sets in, you don’t feel like talking. When the market closes and the sales go well, it’s exciting to return home. That’s when you buy beef or some clothes for your wife waiting at home. Do you understand? “Yes.”

So the Unification Church trains like that. Moreover, that’s how men are. For example, when the Unification Church goes out to evangelize, even if they can’t undergo prison training, they must undergo similar training, so they send everyone out to evangelize without money. This is official.

You have to go and figure it out for yourself. It’s shocking when you get food, but it’s exciting when you have to figure it out on your own. Do you understand? It’s like a secret inspector coming down to investigate or doing a survey of the local sentiment. It’s a special mission.

If Unification Church youth go down to the neighborhood and sacrifice and serve to save that neighborhood, but there are those who oppose them, they could end up succeeding later on... Who was the one who made Chunhyang suffer in the past? “Byeonsato.” They could become like Byeonsato.

To do that, you have to become a beggar and say, “Let’s find out about the character of the people in this neighborhood. It’s lunchtime; please show some kindness.” If you open your eyes wide, they will give you food. You can’t say, “Oh, please give me food.” You have to humbly say, “Um! I’m hungry; please give me some food.” If you do it with authority, they will give you food. There’s a technique to getting food. You have to learn all those laws.

When I go somewhere to get food, I have confidence that I can get food even from a lady who says she won’t give me any. (Laughter) If she doesn’t give it to me, I can see that she has some issues with her father-in-law or that her husband is likely to cheat on her, and then she will end up giving me food. (Laughter) That could happen.

If I see a lady carrying a basket of food, I might follow her and say, “Ma’am, you walk with such grace.” (Laughter) Then she might say, “Really?” I could say, “Looking at your face, you have this kind of fortune, but because you walk like this, you might struggle a bit in your youth, but in your later years, it will be like this.” Then she might say, “Oh, really?” and be happy. Is that possible? Then I would respond, “What food are you bringing?” And she might say, “I’m bringing barley rice or something.” I could then say, “Oh, that sounds like bad food!”—even if it’s not good at that time. I would say, “What I said must be correct.” Then if she says, “No, it’s not,” I could say, “What do you mean it’s not? Let’s see.” And then I could say, “Wow, this looks delicious,” and I could get to eat that food. (Laughter) If you do that, you can get food as much as you want. And it’s not a bad feeling. “Ah, that man is charming! I wish my husband were like that.” 

So, if you’re going to get food, what kind of husband would you want? Even if you become thin from hunger, you think, “She’s carrying a basket of food. I want to eat, but can I? Out of pride, I can’t ask for anything.” What does it mean to be a man? You have to be full. When you have to run a thousand miles, you need to eat to run. You have to eat even if it’s on the road. “Why should I eat? I should just ask for it.” That kind of attitude is necessary. Do you understand?

Sometimes, when the old men in the neighborhood gather and drink, they have snacks... At that time, you ask, “Grandpa, what do you have for snacks?” There’s definitely something there. If you do that, they might say, “What do you mean?” They might say, “I saw something there.” “What did you see?” You say, “Quick, look over here.” Then you put the snack in your mouth and eat it. Is that possible? If I want to eat, I eat like that. Even the old man who was drinking would stop drinking. That training is necessary. Without that kind of play, you can’t make a revolution.

The path of hardship makes you feel the value of life
That’s why when people like us go to prison, within three days, we can make everyone in prison into a mess. I quickly talk to them, saying, “Hey, what’s your home like? Since your situation looks like that, your fate is going to be tough.” After saying that once, if I push them, how can they... “You know that well, don’t you? Right?” “Yes.” Just three phrases like that, and they say, “Oh, Teacher!” That’s necessary.

To save the nation, you have to make the women at home come out; you can’t have the young men go in. To do that, you have to play the game of getting married. Isn’t that right? In order to save the nation, when you’re running with a special mission, you have to do things that can help the nation. Do you understand what I’m saying? “Yes.” That’s what makes the Unification Church different from ordinary churches.

Teacher Moon of the Unification Church doesn’t leave young people alone. He trains them just like I did. And does that make them foolish? Does it make them fail? They absolutely do not fail. They don’t become foolish.

Even when I go abroad, whether it’s France or Italy, especially in places like Italy, I have two interpreters with me, but I make them laugh. When I laugh out loud, they become curious. Since interpreting takes twice as long, it takes about ten minutes. So, everything passes, and after the event, the music starts. But the music is louder than during the event. (There’s a brief moment of silence in the recording)

When I meet the ladies, I also teach them how to manage a household. “You have to treat your husband like this...,” saying, “On cold days, do this, and on hot days, do that, and in spring, do this, and in autumn, do this.” I thought of all those things. Look, would God make a man who is to marry a woman incompetent? It’s not that you’re going out just to meet one woman. And can’t you handle a man who is a bit clumsy? You can do it. If you don’t have the confidence to mold a person who has lived their whole life in that position as you wish, then you cannot guide God according to your desires.

From that perspective, when young men and women go to the local area and endure hardships, it’s not a bad thing; it’s good. When they feel that value and realize that there’s no other way to find a worthwhile life, that’s when...
That road is meant to be taken, isn't it? Will you go or not? 
You have to go.
Today, I mistook our Unification Church mobilization team for college students. 
I may not give much money, but changing clothes and becoming a gentleman can happen in a day. Do you understand? A beggar can become a gentleman in a few hours. 
However, a gentleman can never become a beggar, no matter how long it takes. Do you understand what I mean?
So, when we ask who succeeds there, it is the person who has paved the way for both the beggar to become a gentleman and the gentleman to become a beggar. Such a person can win against both the talented and the untalented. How about that?
Unification Church's Reverend Moon, if he just changes his clothes and goes to the labor site, he is a top worker. At that time, he jokes around saying, "Hey, you rascal!" If you nudge him with your foot, he responds, "Hey, you rascal, what are you doing?" and then you become friends. I can pave all the paths I can live on within this realm. I am doing this to create such people because I have played such games. Then, you will not fail.
Moreover, when you go out to evangelize, how many such things happen? If you go to a place like Gangwon-do, you will see cornfields lined up and many melon fields. You go to those cornfields and loudly shout, "Is there a master here?" and say, "I am just a passing guest, so I will take three ears of corn." (laughter) If the master didn’t hear, at least the neighbors heard, or if not, even the neighborhood dogs heard. 
When the master comes, you say, "Oh, you are the master, but didn’t you hear that? Then you have no right to be a master. You deserve to be robbed." This is how you confront them. And then you laugh and say, "Well, young man, since I met the master, as a passing guest, I will speak honestly. Uncle, I will be here for a few days, so I will take about twenty." and you take it and put it in your bag. What can you do about that? The master should feel good about it. "That young man, right! A man should be like that." That’s what they say. Try it and see if it’s not true. A man should be like that to succeed.
If a young man does that, they would think, "Hey, I wish we could have him as our son-in-law. We should have such a guy as our grandson-in-law. Hey, come here. Come here." If they are someone with a purpose, they would invite him into their inner room. (laughter)
Shall I tell you a funny story? I went to someone’s engagement and ate all the party rice cakes. I ate several bags of rice cakes. If I want to eat, I should eat. If I want to do it, I will do it. The teacher is a man who says he will take on the world. What can’t he do? Reverend Moon of the Unification Church can do anything. Even in running, he has never placed below third. Whatever I decide to do, I must be first.
Those who cannot love their country cannot love heaven.
When I was in high school, I was a wrestling champion. Don’t underestimate me. If I go, my hidden skills will show. I should teach you how to protect yourself. If you are busy, you should grab and throw them off. I have trained for all that. Do you understand? "Yes." Why? Is it because I want to live well? "No." Though my face looks like this, it is to save the country and the world…. If enemies or villains block the way, I must go even if I have to kick them aside. If the path to go is set, I must absolutely go. 
That doesn’t mean I should kill. You shouldn’t kill. Such conviction is necessary.
So, I want to make you useful and wonderful men and women. However, those who keep dodging and making excuses must be beaten to death. (laughter) Why are you laughing? I will not forgive those who hinder the cause of the nation and the world.
Did Reverend Moon of the Unification Church want to go to prison? Why did he go to prison? There was food at home. And my parents loved me more than anyone else. As I said earlier, they truly loved me. When I suddenly disappeared during the Japanese occupation, it was because I was in prison. Do you understand? Right? Huh? You must understand that the members of the Unification Church are those who wish to take responsibility on behalf of this nation and this people. Do you understand? "Yes." The Unification Church must undergo restoration through indemnity. Without restoration through indemnity, responsibility cannot be fulfilled.

You are confused. If you were told to go out and fight for the country and you fought, do you think you have become qualified to fight for the country? Not a chance. You are all just Satan's children. These people come here and say, "Still, I am a loyal subject fighting for my country." What kind of loyal subject are you? You cannot even appear in that position, nor do you have the qualifications to attend that position.

The only reason you can attend that position is that the teacher has allowed you to participate. The teacher says, "Do this. Believe in my words. Since Adam fell by distrusting God, you should be trusted from a position better than Adam. Since Adam could not unite with God and perished, you should unite and go out and fight." That is when restoration through indemnity occurs.

When thinking about this, can you stand in a sacrificial position representing the nation on the path to the establishment of the heavenly kingdom with that kind of appearance? Is it because you are dignified? Not a chance. How can you raise your head and criticize the Unification Church on that subject? Not a chance. Such a person will be eternally caught. God will not carry out the restoration providence with such people. Not a chance.

Throw away all those decadent thoughts. And still call yourselves members of the Unification Church? The members of the Unification Church that the teacher knows are not those kinds of people. Even if you are beaten with a stick until your bones break, you should naturally attend. "I cannot even stand in this position, and even if I did, I would only defile the holy altar, but today, since I have been invited to the heavenly banquet, I will repay that grace." You must do that. Only then will you at least get to eat some bread, and the master will see, "I invited that person, but I am not disappointed." On that subject, how can you raise your head and flirt? Watch whether such a person perishes or not. That person cannot remain in the Unification Church. The teacher is not someone who manages such a group. Because it is impossible to carry out the history of restoration through indemnity with such a group, they will automatically fall away.

That is why you must understand the will of the church and participate in the amazing glory of returning the nation and the world... In this brief life of mine, which has only happened once in history, this moment shines brightly; it does not remain tedious. It will pass. Time does not wait for you. You must wait for the time and match it; time does not come to you and adjust to you. Therefore, when the time comes, you must invest all your sincerity into it. If you know that and waste your time, no one will take responsibility for that. Do you think the teacher will take responsibility? You must understand that.

The teacher who guides you is not a casual teacher who is just going along. He is a serious man. When he knows that the time has come, he does not know whether he will live or die. If he misses that day, the heavens and earth will perish, and with that serious heart, he is trying to resolve this matter, yet you criticize and blame him? Watch and see if you remain. Those people will fall away without a sound, just like the seasons change without them knowing, and through the process of erosion, they will all roll away without a trace. That is the Unification Church.

To undergo restoration through indemnity, offerings are needed, and to make offerings, people are needed. Do you have conditional objects? Did you offer for your family, for your country, or for the world? Depending on that, the conditional objects will differ. In other words, it depends on whether it is the conditional object for individual restoration, family restoration, tribal restoration, national restoration, or world restoration. The person is the same, but the conditions differ. The periods also differ.
We must certainly recognize that we are the descendants of fallen ancestors who cannot transcend the historicity of water and cannot leap beyond it. Only after the restoration through indemnity and the resolution of grievances can the division of responsibility begin. The division of responsibility that leaves behind grievances has caused God to suffer, and we must understand that humanity has not yet encountered a global moment to fulfill this division of responsibility, which is why the history of grievances has been repeated. You need to clearly understand how to overcome the peak of this heavy responsibility. Do you understand?  
340   The Division of Responsibility that Leaves Behind Grievances  
"Yes."  
Why must we restore through indemnity? It is to fulfill the division of responsibility. Why must we fulfill the division of responsibility? It is to resolve the many grievances of history. On the day we complete the division of responsibility, will God's grievances be resolved or not? "They will be resolved." Will humanity's grievances be resolved or not? "They will be resolved." Moreover, even the grievances of the era and the grievances of the future will all be resolved.  
If we cannot fulfill our responsibility by the end of the third seven-year course, the people of the Republic of Korea will become slaves.  
Because the history of many grievances remains, we must long for the day of fulfilling the responsibility that can resolve those grievances. We must long for that. We must long for it more than for anyone else. More than a husband loving his wife and a wife loving her husband, more than loving children, we must long for that. Once we resolve that, we need a wife, a husband, children, a family, and a nation-state, don't we? When you understand this and critically examine the path again, have you walked the path of restoration through indemnity centered on your past self?  
If I am struggling in the position of individual restoration, isn't it my greatest hope to welcome the Messiah to meet the day of family restoration? Since that standard is the very standard by which I can achieve family restoration, I must have the heart that I will not have any grievances even if I give my life for it. If I have fulfilled the responsibility of individual restoration, there are those who can teach me the way to walk the path of family restoration, and if I have completed family restoration and fulfilled the division of responsibility, there are those who can teach me the way to walk the path of tribal restoration. If I have completed tribal restoration and fulfilled the division of responsibility, there are those who can open the way to develop into a nation, or a state, or the world. If someone can teach me to leap over the entire pit of grievances all at once, then what would I want to save—my hands, my feet, my bones? I must become someone who can resolve to invest temporarily, which is one of my greatest wishes and fulfillments.  
341  
Through the Unification Church, you must have the historical mission to restore this all at once through indemnity. Isn't the teaching of the Unification Church today to indemnify the heavy history of 7,000 years within this period of seven years and to leap over the grievances that humanity has been in until now? This seven years is indeed a blessed period for us. If we miss this seven years, we will perish, and our intentions will not be established. Therefore, this seven-year period is the time when we can resolve all the rights of life.  
When the day comes that this seven-year period disappears from me, we can only become men and women of grievances. Without going through this seven-year period, there can be no division of responsibility before you. Without going through this seven-year period, we cannot resolve the grievances of God and humanity until now. Only by fulfilling this seven-year period can we liberate our nation and people. If we cannot do this in the first seven-year course, it will be extended into the second seven-year course and the third seven-year course. If we cannot do it by the end of the third seven-year course, this intention, this blessing will not be the blessing of the Republic of Korea or your blessing, but will pass on to the blessings of other nations. Why? Because that is the will of Jesus and the will of Christianity. On that day, the people of the Republic of Korea will become slaves.  
Look. Just as Ham, the son of Noah, became a slave because he could not fulfill his responsibility while being in the position of the blessed Abel, it will surely be the same. If the nation of Israel had killed the physical and spiritual body of Jesus, that nation would have no way to revive, but because there is a spiritual standard left, it can revive, whereas the Korean nation cannot. The Third Israel stands in a conditional position that can invade the spiritual and physical, so this nation will become like a slave. That is the conclusion of the Principle. You must understand the history of Ham. Leaders of the Unification Church who live with the teacher, wake up! What you have done until now in following the teacher and coming out with a purpose cannot be a one-way street. You must receive criticism here. You must receive principled criticism again in a stark manner.  
Is the life you are living for the nation and representing the world? I take no responsibility. No matter how close someone is, I take no responsibility. No matter who from the 36 families who have served the teacher for decades, I cannot take responsibility. In order to fulfill the path of restoration through indemnity for the nation and the world, one must be a leader who voluntarily takes on the suffering path to shorten the path of restoration through indemnity. You must understand this.  
What is wrong must be settled before going to the spiritual world.  
You may not know what the teacher is doing, what he is saying, or why he is saying such things. These days, I am meeting people who say they are doing something in Korea. I have a responsibility to meet a few top people. Regarding the principle of restoration through indemnity... Because I have prayed before God for Christianity and have a responsibility to save Christianity, I will meet some people from Christianity and then meet people from the spiritual world. I will meet people from various religions. They know the laws of heaven. They know how to receive and uphold the teacher of the Unification Church. You will have a time to be educated by such people in the future. When that education comes, you must receive it. There will come a time when you cannot meet the teacher at will. I think that may happen.  
The principle of restoration through indemnity applies to the teacher himself as well. Before I walked the path of restoration through indemnity, I never thought of wanting to appear before God. Those who have not gone through the process of offering do not need support. If one stands in the position of sympathizing with the offering, one cannot offer a true offering. In that sense, when the teacher went to prison, he never prayed, "God, protect me." Such trivial prayers are absolutely not done. Otherwise, it would violate the meaning of the offering. One must sacrifice cleanly and shed blood cleanly. If one becomes a priest who seeks sympathy, it becomes a blasphemy against God. When there is a difficult situation, I cannot do that. "God, I will take responsibility for myself. I do not need sympathy." You must understand that I am a man who comes out with that mindset.  
343  
You cannot fulfill your responsibility without restoration through indemnity. In trying to achieve national restoration through indemnity, it causes the members of the Unification Church to suffer. It pushes them to the brink of death. Go! When the direction you are going is at odds with this direction, you will be judged according to the degree of that divergence. I would rather have not known. Wouldn't it have been better if someone like Judas Iscariot had not known? I would rather have never been born! I would rather have never believed in the Unification Church, or never known the teacher!  
Then, it is not just your lifetime that is at stake; if you are not careful, it will also affect your ancestors up to the 70th generation. If there are good merits, they will all be taken away and given to foreign people. This is not just talk. It is not a spiritual threat to you; the content is such. If, after saying this much, you still do not do it, I do not know. Do you understand? Can you fulfill the division of responsibility before restoration through indemnity? "No!" There is none.  
When has the teacher ever thought about going the path of restoration through indemnity until now? When has he felt or sympathized with the path of restoration through indemnity? Even when a cow is slaughtered for a sacrifice in a village, it is remembered as the village's sacrifice day, and people have compassion for the offering. How much have you sympathized with the teacher? You are all trying to use the teacher and take advantage of him... I will thoroughly investigate this in the future. If the purpose is realized, all the notorious trivial men will be documented and brought to trial to resolve the issues. All the wrongs will be uncovered and resolved. Why? Because judgment is historical.  
From the past to the present and future, we will trace who has done wrong and compile records, and all those lineages will be uncovered and settled. If there are pastors who oppose the Unification Church, they will all be caught. The man who stands in the position to walk that path is the teacher of the Unification Church. It cannot be passed over lightly.  
Words that have shocked my heart, words I did not say, where did they come from? I must cleanly organize all the roots of these things. If I cannot do that on this earth, I must settle it cleanly even in the spiritual world. When settling in the spiritual world, there will be no way to forgive them forever. Why? Because they do not forgive... You must understand this. You must understand the division of responsibility that leaves behind grievances.  
Fulfill your responsibility as the subject nation of faith.  
Therefore, you must ask yourself, has this hand fulfilled the division of responsibility? How much has this hand worked to fulfill the division of responsibility? When viewed this way, this hand must be detestable. You must have the heart that wants to smash this hand! This eye! This mouth! What do you want to open your mouth for? This mouth! You must have the desire to take an axe and smash your teeth to pieces. Even if you resolve to smash all your fingers like a bat smashing a snake's head, you must think it is not a waste. Just because the lump of flesh is struggling, does that mean it is difficult? You cannot restore through indemnity with that attitude.  
Now, you know this, and the question of how to ascend the path of the division of responsibility that leaves behind grievances is a new task. How will you push this forward in this period of just over two years until 1974? If this period passes, the era of national mission will be over. Do you understand what I mean? The teacher of the Unification Church does not say to you, "Do this, do that. Hey, evangelize." He absolutely does not say that. If you want to do it, do it; if you don’t, then don’t... I have nothing to do with it. At that time, the teacher of the Unification Church may be in a place where you cannot see him. What I am saying is not my words.  
Young maidens and young men, as well as older people, must all go the path of restoration through indemnity. Day and night, you must bear the fate of crying out and wrestling with the world, because you are members of the Unification Church, and the path to resolve the grievances left behind is the path we started on to overcome the peak of the division of responsibility that leaves behind grievances. If we do not completely overcome this path victoriously, the fate of the Unification Church will be a miserable fate. The grip of the communist world that is binding us is currently prevailing in the world, isn't it?  
You must understand this and clearly discern that the second seven-year course until 1974 is the period you must take responsibility for. You must expand the responsibility you have to take for your family to the nation. Therefore, you must connect with 777 families worldwide, and those families are all coordinating with you.  
If you become one who loses to them, you will stand in a position where you cannot fulfill your responsibility as the subject nation.  
<Prayer> Father! This son standing here, from the day I understood your will, I recall every moment of determination I made, thinking about the path of restoration that is a long journey of a thousand miles. Since that day when I could not speak to anyone about the sorrowful inner feelings of the father, I have waited for the time of heaven to come with a deep heart.  
During that time, I have passed through my youth and my young adult years, and now I have reached a point where I must face the sunset path. Now, as I witness the nation and the world becoming chaotic, I feel the historical significance I bear in common with God. Each time I feel that way, I feel guilty, and when I start my daily life, I see that my heart is filled with concern for this nation and the world, and I cannot help but feel that the time of heaven is drawing near.  
However, O Heaven! Please remember this pitiful Korean nation. This nation that has passed through a history of five millennia, this nation that has lived in a position like a sorrowful orphan, this nation that has endured humiliation like the child of a beggar, still believes that God exists and, when it is cold, turns its heart to long for parents, praying, "Our parents have died, but God, please help us." You know that this is the historical connection left by the Korean people, and because you know this, you have come to find this nation and wanted to give it a blessing that can endure through many hardships, but this nation has betrayed you.  
Father! I know that you have a heart that forgives the nation of Israel, and I see that your unjust will remains in not destroying Judaism, and I feel how regretful it is today that I must pray before you with this in mind. However, the path of restoration that cannot be fulfilled, the path that can be fulfilled repeatedly, is not our will but your will, and when I think that we must fulfill this mission before we die, I must have the heart to hope for a victorious time when we can be recognized before you again, and this is the nationalistic thought and pride of being born as a nation, Father, please forgive us.  
Father, the Unification Church has walked the path of suffering through adversity since liberation. We have endured grievances that cannot be spoken of to anyone. Even in the face of grinding teeth or strained tendons, we have endured while thinking of your sorrowful days. We know that we must become those whom you can eternally boast of, and we hope and desire that you love this nation and this people.  
Who will take the initiative for the divided unification of the North and South? We know that only God can take responsibility for this. We are insufficient, so we must become a miserable group that can block this sorrowful fate and be prepared to bear the cross of death. Every time we think of this, we quietly long for your embrace, hoping for the results of the day of victory you establish, and we must break through this difficult situation, which is the current mission of the Unification Church, and we earnestly hope and desire that everyone’s heart will firmly believe this.  
Father, this year is 1972. This year can represent a historical misery. The events that occur this year are not only the history of the Korean people but also represent the history of the world.  
As October approaches, this nation and this people have declared a state of emergency. At this time, what should we be looking at? The more things are like this, the deeper God's heart becomes...
We must delve into the heart of love.  
Heaven! Please do not forsake this nation, and love this country and its people.  
I know there must be a group that is determined to leave behind this intention, even if we have to sacrifice.  
The children gathered here today have realized the heavy responsibility we bear, and I ask that we be allowed to become a group that clearly understands we must walk the path of indemnity and restoration to complete this.  
At this time, I earnestly request and hope that it becomes a time to renew our loyalty and pledge before the Father.  
Father, even if we stand at a weary and exhausted place as we approach the final stages of this path we must walk until 1974, we must not rest until we have stepped over even one step toward the summit, risking our lives. The more difficult it becomes, the more we must recognize that we are getting closer to the summit and be determined to overcome. Please allow us to be like true warriors who can overcome, and let the children of heaven show their perseverance and strength in the satanic world, becoming the workers of unification who lack nothing because of Your love.  
At this time, as we gather our minds and bodies, looking toward the hope of tomorrow, I earnestly ask that each of us solemnly pledge and become aware before the Father, and I humbly present all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
